# 3.2 UlData

## 3.2.1 General UlData

**3.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11513637`)

General UlData
Description: UL data transfer

Used by: 5G-L2-PS, 5G-L2-LO

Addressing: 5G\_L1\_IF\_14428\_replaced([11515396](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR8H5PvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.2.1.1 UlData Interface Principles

**3.2.1.1.0-4**  (ID: `11513654`)

UlData Interface Principles
[Before CNI-98319]

For Loki-L1-HW [RP003187-A] and Thor-L1-HW [End RP003187-A] only, 5G-L1-UL shall use information from msgCountCtrl IE (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_113\_replaced([11513182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRuskPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from arriving UlData\_\*ReceiveReq messages to trigger datapath processing before end of the reception window (value B) specified under 5G\_L1\_IF\_276\_replaced([11514719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5EnPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before PR591229]

msgCountCtrl IE contains following information:

* lastMsg (1 bit, boolean): True for the last UlData\_\*ReceiveReq sent by the 5G-L2-PS (UL or DL) scheduler for a given subcell/slot; False for other requests.
* lastMsgCount (3 bits): number of messages with lastMsg set to True in a given subcell/slot. Depends on the number of active schedulers in a given subcell/slot.
* msgCount (4 bits): valid only when lastMsg is True. Contains total count of UlData\_\*ReceiveReq messages that were scheduled by the UL or DL scheduler for a given subcell/slot.

[End PR591229]

[PR591229]

msgCountCtrl IE contains following information:

* lastMsg (1 bit, boolean): True for the last UlData\_\*ReceiveReq sent by the 5G-L2-PS (UL or DL) scheduler for a given subcell/slot; False for other requests.
* lastMsgCount (2 bits): number of messages with lastMsg set to True in a given subcell/slot. Depends on the number of active schedulers in a given subcell/slot.
* msgCount (5 bits): valid only when lastMsg is True. Contains total count of UlData\_\*ReceiveReq messages that were scheduled by the UL or DL scheduler for a given subcell/slot.

[End PR591229]

Upon receiving UlData\_\*ReceiveReq message, 5G-L1-UL shall:

- Count messages with lastMsg = True up to lastMsgCount.

5G-L1-UL can assume that msgLastCount is the same across all received messages in a given subcell/slot.

- Count messages up to Y, where Y is the sum of msgCount over all messages with lastMsg = True.

- If number of received messages is equal to Y, then 5G-L1-UL shall trigger datapath processing

Note:

* If there is no UL channel/signal to be sent for a subcell/slot from DL or UL scheduler(s), 5G-L2-PS sends UlData\_EmptyReceiveReq message with msgCountCtrl IE filled as follows:
* lastMsg = True
* lastMsgCount set as in other messages
* msgCount = 1
* If UlData\_EmptyReceiveReq acts as a replacement message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_260\_replaced([11514555](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32gvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then msgCountCtrl IE in this message is filled as follows:
* lastMsg = True
* lastMsgCount set as in other messages
* msgCount = number of UL channel/signal sent from DL or UL scheduler including UlData\_EmptyReceiveReq.

[CNI-98319]

msgCountCtrl IE is removed from UlData\_\*ReceiveReq messages.

[End CNI-98319]

---

## 3.2.2 Uplink Addressing Procedure

**3.2.2.0-7**  (ID: `11513688`)

Uplink Addressing Procedure
**UlData\_AddressResp message content:**

| cause | enum{ 0: NoError 1: InvalidSubcellId 2: SubcellNotExist 3: UlStartupIncomplete} | Cause of status 0: No error 1: SubcellId is invalid 2: SubcellId is valid, but subcell does not exist 3: UL Startup is incomplete | **Loner/Loki/Thor:** enum{ 0: NoError 1: InvalidSubcellId 2: SubcellNotExist 3: UlStartupIncomplete} | [1] [2] | CB008375-A |

**Invalid combinations**

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Index** | **Invalid combination** | **Note** |
| [1] | status = 0(OK) AND cause > 0 | when status = 0(OK), cause should = 0(NoError) |
| [2] | status = 1(NOK) AND cause = 0(NoError) | when status = 1(NOK), cause should > 0 |

Note \*: Here u8[0...7] for Loner means L1sw on Loner will fetch lowest 8bits of this parameter.

**[CB009028-5G-A] Parity from CB008249:**

This requirement also applies to Thor.

**[End CB009028-5G-A]**

**[CNI-122313]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313]**

## 3.2.3 Synchronization Procedures

### 3.2.3.0-2 Synchronization Procedures Synchronization of System Frame Number (SFN) GPS signal is connected to ASIA board and under responsibility of platform Platform has to provide BCN (base station clock number) according to the ToD (Time of Day) of GPS signal BCN in ASIA board will be set accordingly and goes via RP1 synchronization burst to all ABIK boards (L1) of the 5GNB (ID: 11513701)

General
Expected Exceptions:

Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

(see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3324([11150688: CFO metric - Exponential average](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksVDQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3333([11151157: LT CFO validity for PUSCH/PUCCH](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3337([11151189: LT CFO validity for RACH Msg3](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).   **[CNI-78025]** Applicable for Loner, and Loki.   To help L2-PS to maintain features 2RX, 4RX, 8RX ; L1 PUSCH shall ensure LT CFO protection for reception of 0+j0 from L2-PS, - For L2-PS, when using 0+j0 for LT CFO reset, no validity check is performed anymore (i.e., not modify value 0 to 1.0 in purpose). - For L1SW, assume frequency offset equals 0Hz if LT CFO == 0+j0 is received. | >>longTermCfoMetricOfBeam | array [4] complex | **For C8 [CB013442-D] and A8 [End CB013442-D] subcell only: Long term CFO metric is sent for each beam. Each value corresponds to two continuous Rx antenna streams and L1 shall duplicate it internally after receiving from L2-PS.**   The mapping relationship is given as: -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] ceAxC [0] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] ceAxC [1] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] ceAxC [2] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] ceAxC [3] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] ceAxC [4] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] ceAxC [5] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] ceAxC [6] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] ceAxC [7]   ceAxC[2i+1] has the same value as ceAxC[2i] with i = 0,1,2,3. L1 shall duplicate the values to fit 8 ceAxC streams internally.   **For all other cases (not C8 subcell): Long term CFO metric is sent for each Rx stream. Each value corresponds to one Rx antenna stream.**   The mapping relationship is given as: -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0]: (ce)AxC [0] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1]: (ce)AxC [1] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2]: (ce)AxC [2] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3]: (ce)AxC [3]   In 2Rx case, the last two elements are set as invalid values.   5G-L1-UL shall ensure LT CFO protection for reception of 0+0j from 5G-L2-PS. - For L2-PS, when using 0+j0 for LT CFO reset, no validity check is performed anymore (i.e., not modify value 0 to 1.0 in purpose). - For L1SW, assume frequency offset equals 0Hz if LT CFO == 0+j0 is received. Note: it is also possible that only some beams (i.e., two of total four) have LT CFO == 0+j0, while other antennas have non-zero values. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9896.   [Before PR831459-25R3] **[CB010708-D] Note: in eCPRI 7-2e, 5G-L1-UL shall check the field in message UlData\_PuschReceivReqL1Ru for longTermCfoMetricOfBeam configuration** **[End CB010708-D]** **[PR831459-25R3]** Note: In eCPRI 7-2e split, 5G-L2-PS shall set this parameter longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0~3]  to the top 4 best beams. For MU\_MIMO case, 5G-L2-PS only combines the channel metric from a given UE's own beams, sets the rest of longTermCfoMetricOfBeam to 0. **3.2.4.1.2.0-1.0-10**  (ID: `12884359`)

PUSCH Receive Request message
**eCpriConfig**

**[CB008577-C]**

Important note: This structure replaced the old common **eCpriConfig structure ([11514653](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dkfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**[End CB008577-C]**

| **Thor:** u8{2,4,6,8} **Odin :** **[CB012115-IA]** u8{2,4,6,8} **[End CB012115-IA]** **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: u8 {2,4}** **[End CB016075-K]** |  |  |  |  |
| >>ceAxcIndex | array[8] of u8 [0..numCeAxCId-1] | Set of eAxC indices to be used for the given channel/signal reception for this grant on eCPRI Fronthaul. See [11513650](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRyW4fvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) for ceAxcIndex. Only first numCeAxcIndex are valid. | **Loner/Loki:** array[4] of u8 [0..numCeAxCId-1] | 5GC000399-KX 5GC001868-A RP003187-A CB012115-IA |
| **Thor:** array[8] of u8 [0..numCeAxCId-1] **Odin :** **[CB012115-IA]** array[8] of u8 [0..numCeAxCId-1] **[End CB012115-IA]** **[CB016075-K]** **GPU:** array[8] of u8 [0..numCeAxCId-1] **[End CB016075-K]** |  |  |  |  |
| >>patternId | array[4] of u16 | beam patternIds to be used for given channel/signal reception for this grant, and the eCPRI control message generation. Each patternId is used with two consecutive ceAxcIndex.   In case of 4Rx, only the first two elements are valid. The last two elements are filled in with invalid values (0x0000). | **Loner/Loki/Thor:** array[2] of u16 | 5GC000399-KX 5GC001868-A RP003187-A CB012115-IA |
| **Thor:** **[Before CB009363-A]** array[2] of u16 **[CB009363-A]** array[4] of u16 **[End CB009363-A]** **Odin :** **[CB012115-IA]** array[4] of u16 **[End CB012115-IA]** **[CB016075-K]** **GPU:** array[4] of u16 **[End CB016075-K]** |  |  |  |  |
| >>suSplitpanelMode | array[4] of u8 | Indicator of the split-panel mode used in FDD A8 8Rx PUSCH SU MIMO IRC receiver. All elements have a one-one mapping relationship with their counterparts in patternId. For each element, the value corresponds to a specific TRX panel split mode. 0: full panel 9: 1x4, 1st from left 10: 1x4, 2nd from left 11: 1x4, 3rd from left 12: 1x4, 4th from left For detailed usage, refer to chapter 4.2.2.2.9 of <> ([12739988](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SQ7TEHnCEfCiUemk-K-C4g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). If not FDD A8 8Rx PUSCH SU MIMO IRC receiver, the field shall be ignored by 5G-L1-UL and all elements are 0. | **Loner/Loki: Not supported** Thor: array[4] of u8 **[CB016075-K]** **GPU:** Not supported **[End CB016075-K]** | CB008577-C |

**3.2.4.1.3.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `11513856`)

PUSCH Receive Response Ps message
UCI on PUSCH Dtx metrics and Thresholds

---

**3.2.4.1.3.0-1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11513859`)

PUSCH Receive Response Ps message
Dtx metrics and Thresholds for the decisions are reported as dtxThresholdCsiPart1, dtxThresholdAck1Bit, dtxThresholdCsiPart2 in the tables below*.*

Metrics are defined as:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Number of bits** | dtxMetricCsiPart1 | dtxMetricAck1Bit | dtxMetricAckMoreThan1Bit | dtxMetricCsiPart2 |
| **1 or 2 bits** | Not needed | **[5GC000885-A] Q0.13.3**   **[CB006064-A] Q0.13.3** | **[5GC000885-E] Q0.13.3** **[CB006064-A] Q0.13.3** | Not needed |
| **[3..11] (Reed- Muller coding)** | **[5GC000885-E]Q0.13.3** | Not needed | **[CB006064-A] Q0.13.3** ~~[5GC000885-C]~~ ~~xxxx~~ | **[5GC001817-A/CB007220-A] Q0.13.3** |
| **[12..19]** **(Polar Coding)** | **[CB006064-E]  Q0.16.0** | Not needed | Not needed | **[5GC001817-B/CB007220-B] Q0.16.0** |
| **Equal or higher than 20 bits** **(Polar Coding)** | **[CB006064-E]**Q0.16.0\*\*\*\* | Not needed | Not needed | Not needed yet |

Thresholds are defined as:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Number of bits** | dtxThresholdCsiPart1 | dtxThresholdAck1Bit | dtxThresholdAckMoreThan1Bit | dtxThresholdCsiPart2 |
| **1 or 2 bits** | Not needed | **[5GC000885-A] Q0.5.11** **[CB006064-A] Q0.5.11** | **[5GC000885-E] Q0.5.11** **[CB006064-A] Q0.5.11** | Not needed |
| **[3..11] (Reed- Muller coding)** | **[5GC000885-E]Q0.13.3** | Not needed | **[CB006064-A] Q0.13.3** ~~[5GC000885-C]~~ ~~xxxx~~ | **[5GC001817-A/CB007220-A] Q0.13.3** |
| **[12..19]** **(Polar Coding)** | **[CB006064-E]**Q0.0.16\*\*\*\* | Not needed | Not needed | **[5GC001817-B/CB007220-B] Q0.0.16** |
| **Equal or higher than 20 bits** **(Polar Coding)** | **[CB006064-E]**Q0.0.16\*\*\*\* | Not needed | Not needed | Not needed yet |

Where Q0.X.Y means unsigned number with:

X: number of bits for the integer part

Y: number of bits for the fractional part

~~Number of UCI bits can be determined from the~~ ~~numOfBitsOfUciInformation~~~~of~~ ~~UlData\_PuschReceiveReq~~~~.~~

**[CNI-122313]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313]**

[CB012115-IA] Odin shall support this structure in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs message, on par with Thor, in terms of the information elements and their supported ranges. [End CB012115-IA]

**3.2.4.1.3.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `11513864`)

PUSCH Receive Response Ps message
**PuschUciBitsResp:**

This structure is used in **UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs message.**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| >>uciCsiPart1Bits | array [6] u8 **[5GC001817-B] array [7 ]u8** [end 5GC001817-B]\*\*\*\* | CSI part 1 bits of UCI report.   Valid entries correspond to indexes from 0 to numOfUciCsiPart1Bits - 1. Bits are filled from the MSB to LSB and padding bits are located on the least significant bits of the last octet. If number of UCI bits is lower than 8, padding bits are also set on least significant bits of first octet.   See example in the below.   For supported values, see 5G\_L1\_7652\_replaced([11405805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9aSf_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loner/Loki/Thor/Odin[CB016075-K]/GPU[End CB016075-K]:** array u8[7] |  | 5GC000885-E ~~5GC001817-B~~ ~~5GC001969~~-B |
| >>csiPart1CrcCheck | u8{0=Pass, 1=Fail} | When the number of CSI Part 1 bits is higher than 11 bit. The check is performed. If there are less than or equal to 11 bits, the IE is ignored by L2-Ps | **Loner/Loki/Thor/Odin[CB016075-K]/GPU[End CB016075-K]:** u8{0,1} |  | 5GC001817-A |
| >>numOfUciCsiPart2Bits | u8~~[0..5]~~ ~~[CB007220-B]~~ ~~u8[0..16]~~ ~~[End CB007220-B]~~ | Number of CSI bits (part 2) in UCI report.     For supported values, see 5G\_L1\_5453\_replaced([11406332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9cutfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loner/Loki/Thor/Odin:** [1..3] **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: u8{0}** **[End CB016075-K]** |  | 5GC001817-A CB007220-A |
| >>uciCsiPart2Bits | array [7] of u8 | CSI part 2 bits of UCI report.   Valid entries correspond to indexes from 0 to numOfUciCsiPart2Bits - 1. Bits are filled from the MSB to LSB and padding bits are located on the least significant bits of the last octet. If number of UCI bits is lower than 8, padding bits are also set on least significant bits of first octet.   See example in the below with CSI1. | **Loner/Loki/Thor/Odin:** array [7] of u8   **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: Not supported** **[End CB016075-K]** |  | 5GC001817-A CB007220-A |
| >>csiPart2CrcCheck | u8{0=Pass, 1=Fail} | When the number of CSI Part 2 bits is higher than 11 bit, the check is performed. If there are less than or equal to 11 bits, the IE is ignored by L2-Ps | **Loner/Loki/Thor/Odin:** u8{0,1} **[CB016075-K]** **GPU: Not supported** **[End CB016075-K]** |  | 5GC001817-A CB007220-A |

Remark: The IEs are explained in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1035

uciCsiPart1Bits example with 4 bit CSI1:

csi1\_0=1

csi1\_1=1

csi1\_2=1

csi1\_3=0

uciCsiPart1Bits[6]  : xxxx xxxxx

uciCsiPart1Bits[5]  : xxxx xxxxx

uciCsiPart1Bits[4]  : xxxx xxxxx

uciCsiPart1Bits[3]  : xxxx xxxxx

uciCsiPart1Bits[2]  : xxxx xxxxx

uciCsiPart1Bits[1]  : xxxx xxxxx

uciCsiPart1Bits[0]  : 1110 xxxxx

**[CNI-122313]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313]**

[CB012115-IA] Odin shall support this structure in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs message, on par with Thor, in terms of the information elements and their supported ranges. [End CB012115-IA]

#### 3.2.4.1.4 PUSCH Receive Response Lo message

##### 3.2.4.1.4.0-1 PUSCH Receive Response Lo message Loki/Thor/vRAN/Odin/GPU (ID: 11513872)

**3.2.4.1.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11513875`)

PUSCH Receive Response Lo message
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo message content:**

**[CNI-132817]**

**Important note: The old UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages. On Loner platforms,****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15435\_replaced([11513883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlDPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoL1sw. Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoLoner or****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoL1sw message definition should be used.*****\*******\*******\*******\****

**UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoL1sw message content:**

**[End CNI-132817]**

[CB012115-IA] Odin shall support this message, on par with Thor, in terms of the information elements and their supported ranges. [End CB012115-IA]

##### 3.2.4.1.4.0-2 PUSCH Receive Response Lo message Loner (ID: 11513881)

**3.2.4.1.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11513883`)

PUSCH Receive Response Lo message
**[CNI-132817]**

**Important note: The old UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages. On Loner platforms,****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoLoner and on all other platforms****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_208\_replaced([11513875](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlCvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoLoner or****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoL1sw message definition should be used.*****\*******\*******\*******\****

**UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoLoner message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |

| slot | u8[0..79] | NR-slot (38.211 §4.3.2) | **Loner:** u8[0..79] |  |  |

| bufferedUlRespLoner | Structure, see separate definition in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15496\_replaced([11514666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5EkPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | In case of buffered subcell, contains SFN and slot numbers of the slot when the channel was processed. Variables defined in this structure are directly listed in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLoLoner message. | **Loner:** See 5G\_L1\_IF\_15496\_replaced([11514666](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5EkPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) |  | 5GC001120-A 5GC001120-B |

Note: when no fragmentation (i.e. totalFragmentNum==0 or totalFragmentNum==1) fragmentSizeBytes is the size of the transport block in byte. | **Loner:** u32 |  | 5GC001118-A 5GC001118-B RP003187-E |
| fragmentIndex | u8 [0.. totalFragmentNum-1] | The fragment index in the transport block. Note: When totalFragmentNum==0 or totalFragmentNum==1, fragmentIndex is always 0. | **Loner:** u8 [0.. 7-1] |  | 5GC001118-A 5GC001118-B RP003187-E |
| totalFragmentNum | u8 [0..10] | Total number of fragments used to transport this TB. Note: for backward compatibility purposes, value 0 as same meaning as value 1, i.e., no fragmentation means one single fragment. | **Loner:** u8 [0..10] |  | 5GC001118-A 5GC001118-B RP003187-E |
| tbStatus | u8 [0,1] | Positive / negative acknowledgment of the fragmented transport block, - 0 means CRC check passed for this fragment and the previous ones. - 1 means CRC failure in this fragment and then TB failure. | k2 | u8 [0..32] | k2 value received in *UlData\_PuschReceiveReq (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_197\_replaced([11513788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy9_fvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).* On Loner, this field is not filled by L1-FPGA and shall be ignored by L2-LO. | **Loner:** Not supported |  |  |

##### 3.2.4.1.5.0-2 PUSCH Receive Response HarqU message Loner (ID: 11513903)

**3.2.4.1.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11513907`)

PUSCH Receive Response HarqU message
**[CNI-132817]**

**Important note: The old UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqU message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages. On Loner platforms,****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqU continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqULoner and on all other platforms****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqU continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqUL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_209\_replaced([11513897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlD_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqU is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqULoner or****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqUL1sw message definition should be used.*****\*******\*******\*******\****

**UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqULoner message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |

#### 3.2.4.1.6 PUSCH Receive Response HarqD message

##### 3.2.4.1.6.0-1 PUSCH Receive Response HarqD message Loki/Thor/vRAN/Odin/GPU (ID: 11513915)

**3.2.4.1.6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11513919`)

PUSCH Receive Response HarqD message
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD message content:**

**[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD message in Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC001868-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-132817]**

**Important note: The old UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages. On Loner platforms,****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15437\_replaced([11513932](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0ME_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDL1sw. Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDLoner or****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDL1sw message definition should be used.*****\*******\*******\*******\****

**UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDL1sw message content:**

**[End CNI-132817]**

[CB012115-IA] Odin shall support this message, on par with Thor, in terms of the information elements and their supported ranges. [End CB012115-IA]

##### 3.2.4.1.6.0-2 PUSCH Receive Response HarqD message Loner (ID: 11513928)

**3.2.4.1.6.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11513932`)

PUSCH Receive Response HarqD message
**[CNI-132817]**

**Important note: The old UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages. On Loner platforms,****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDLoner and on all other platforms****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD continues as****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDL1sw(see 5G\_L1\_IF\_210\_replaced([11513919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MEPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDLoner or****UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDL1sw message definition should be used.*****\*******\*******\*******\****

[End CNI-132817]

### 3.2.4.2 Physical Uplink Control Channel

**3.2.4.2.0-1**  (ID: `11513945`)

Physical Uplink Control Channel
Document Owner

Dariusz Kobylarz

co-author: Wenjian Li

---

#### 3.2.4.2.1 General

##### 3.2.4.2.1.1 PUCCH messages overview

**3.2.4.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11513958`)

PUCCH messages overview
**Messages:**

UlData\_PucchReceiveReq

UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs

UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD

**Purpose:**

This procedure gives to 5G-L1-UL necessary information to receive and decode each control data scheduled on PUCCH.

**Precondition:**

subcell exists and L1 uplink addresses have been negotiated for it (~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_173~~ 5G\_L1\_IF\_173\_replaced([11513659](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRyW4_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**Triggering condition:**

This procedure is triggered by 5G-L2-PS on a TTI basis to decode data received on PUCCH. The message *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is sent before reception of PUCCH over the air, and various responses are send back to 5G-L2-PS once control data on PUCCH has been decoded.*

**Addressing:**

The request is sent to the pucchReceiveReqAddress of UlData\_AddressResp.

The addresses to send the related responses are given in the request.

**Relevant UP MSCs:**

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_186: Beam Management (TBD)

5G\_L1L2\_FLOW\_259: DL HARQ Tx

~~5G\_RAN\_UP\_525~~: Scheduling Request (SR)

**[CB012115-IA] The above requirement shall be supported in L1 Odin**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

[CB016075-K] The above messages shall be supported by L1 GPU. [End CB016075-K]

---

##### 3.2.4.2.1.2 PUCCH procedures description

**3.2.4.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11513968`)

PUCCH procedures description
11513968:
PUCCH procedures description
11513968:
PUCCH procedures description
11513968:
PUCCH procedures description
The Client is L2-PS (UL & DL scheduler part)

**Description:**

**1: The 5G-L1-UL receives a *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq \*\*message.***\*\*

The message contains a list of PUCCH resources to be decoded, each one is associated to the set of UCI to be decoded.

The message contains a set of addresses for each response message returned to the Client:

* One Client address (EQID) where the message *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs shall be sent*
* One Client address (EQID) where the message *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD shall be sent*

For L2-RT, connectivity is reversed at HWAPI side. L2-RT shall use correct API em\_queue\_create pointing now to L1 instance to communicate with 5G-L1-UL.

**[5GC001626-B, 5GC0000998-A] This procedure shall be done per subcell as there is one subcell per NrCellGrp and each NrCellGrp corresponds to a separate process in L2-RT. This means that IE numSubcell in UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is always set to 1, and 5G-L1-UL sends response messages for each subcell separately.**[End 5GC001626-B, 5GC0000998-A]\*\*\*\*

5G-L1-UL shall receive one *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message for each sub-cell (no aggregation of sub-cells).*

Only one *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message with multiple UEs aggregated shall be received per subcell per slot.*

Only one *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq with multiple formats aggregated shall be received per subcell per slot.*

**NOTE: 5G-L2-PS sends UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message to 5G-L1-UL.**

**2&3: After decoding control data received on PUCCH, the 5G-L1-UL returns a set of metrics to the Client via the message *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs\*\*.***\*\*

This message contains a set of UE specific measurement results dedicated to the Client.

The message is sent to the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsClient address given in the *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message.*

Also the message contains a list of UCI that contains feedback from the UE on measurements made on downlink reference signals.

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate Format0 and Format2 PUCCH resources in one *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.*

5G-L1-UL shall aggregate Format1 and Format3 PUCCH resources in one *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.*

5G-L1-UL shall send one *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message for each sub-cell (no aggregation of sub-cells).*

Only one *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message with multiple UEs aggregated shall be sent per subcell per slot.*

**NOTE:  5G-L1-UL receives UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message from 5G-L2-PS.**

**4. The message *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD **is sent to the Client to the UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDClient address given in the \*UlData\_PucchReceiveReq** message.*****\***

Ack/Nack bits are separated and returned to the Client to handle DL HARQ process.

The transmission of the message *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD to the Client depends on the IE* pucchFormat in the *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message (see ~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1075~~ 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*\*\*

Note:

For configuration with Short PUCCH up to two *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages can be sent per slot if AN reporting is requested on both PUCCH Format 0 and Format 2.*

For configuration with Long PUCCH, up to two *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages can be sent per slot if AN reporting is requested on both PUCCH Format 1 and Format 3.*

5G-L1-UL shall send separate *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message for Format0 and Format2 PUCCH resources (no aggregation for format nor for sub-cell).*

5G-L1-UL shall send separate *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message for Format1 and Format3 PUCCH resources (no aggregation for format nor for sub-cell).*

5G-L1-UL shall send one *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message for each sub-cell (no aggregation of sub-cells).*

For each PUCCH format, 5G-L1-UL shall send only one *UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message with multiple UEs aggregated per slot per sub-cell.*

**[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages and all the related procedures in Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC001868-A]\*\*\*\*

**[5GC001972-A] 5G-L1-UL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages and all the related procedures in vDU L1 HW** [End 5GC001972-A]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] 5G-L1-UL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD messages and all the related procedures in L1 Thor. Note that 5G-L1-UL shall not aggregate Format0 and Format2** [End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The above requirement shall be supported in L1 Odin**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

[CB016075-K] The above messages shall be supported by L1 GPU. [End CB016075-K]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication flow between two entities: "5G L2 PS" and "UL 5G L1".
The diagram shows three messages exchanged between these entities:
1. **1:UIData\_PucchReceiveReq**: This message is sent from "5G L2 PS" to "UL 5G L1".
2. **2:UIData\_PucchReceiveRespPs**: This message is sent from "UL 5G L1" back to "5G L2 PS".
3. **3:UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD (optional)**: This message is also sent from "UL 5G L1" back to "5G L2 PS" and is marked as optional.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_414.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

---

##### 3.2.4.2.1.3 Expected Exceptions

**3.2.4.2.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `11513975`)

Expected Exceptions
**Expected Exceptions:**

**Unexpected Exceptions:**

In case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

**[CB012115-IA] The above requirement shall be supported in L1 Odin**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

[CB016075-K] The above messages shall be supported by L1 GPU. [End CB016075-K]

#### 3.2.4.2.2 PUCCH Receive Request message

##### 3.2.4.2.2.1 PUCCH Receive Request message content

###### 3.2.4.2.2.1.0-1 PUCCH Receive Request message content Loki/Thor/Odin/GPU (ID: 11513986)

**3.2.4.2.2.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11513990`)

PUCCH Receive Request message content
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message content:**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages.**

On Loner platforms, **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq  continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15463\_replaced([11514001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq  continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw.***\****\*

Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner or **UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

**UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw****message content:**\*\*\*\*

| >>longTermCfoMetricOfBeam | StaticFixedSizedArray[4] of complex | For C8, C8'2, C8'4, C8'8 [CB013442-D] and A8 [End CB013442-D]  subcell only: Long term CFO metric is sent for each beam. Each value corresponds to two continuous Rx antenna streams and L1 shall duplicate it internally after receiving from L2-PS.   The mapping relationship is given as: -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] ceAxC [0] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0] ceAxC [1] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] ceAxC [2] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] ceAxC [3] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] ceAxC [4] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[2] ceAxC [5] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] ceAxC [6] -longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[3] ceAxC [7]   ceAxC[2i+1] has the same value as ceAxC[2i] with i = 0,1,2,3. L1 shall duplicate the values to fit 8 ceAxC streams internally.   **Note: If 4Rx PUCCH is configured in C8 or C8'2 or C8'4 or C8'8 subcell, only the first two elements of longTermCfoMetricOfBeam are valid and they corresponds to ceAxC[0-3]. 5G-L1-UL shall expect the last two elements as invalid value.**   **For all other cases (A2, A4, C2, C4 subcell): Long term CFO metric is sent for each Rx stream. ###### 3.2.4.2.2.1.0-2 PUCCH Receive Request message content Loner (ID: 11513997)

**3.2.4.2.2.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11514001`)

PUCCH Receive Request message content
**UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner message**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages.**

On Loner platforms, **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq  continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner(5G\_L1\_IF\_15463\_replaced([11514001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq  continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw(see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*

Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner or **UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

**UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner message content:**

##### 3.2.4.2.2.2 staticLongPucchConfigEcpri structure

###### 3.2.4.2.2.2.1 staticLongPucchConfigEcpri structure content

###### 3.2.4.2.2.2.1.0-1 staticLongPucchConfigEcpri structure content Loki/Thor/GPU (ID: 11514016)

**3.2.4.2.2.2.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11514021`)

staticLongPucchConfigEcpri structure content
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**staticLongPucchConfigEcpri content:**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **staticLongPucchConfigEcpri structure is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**

Into **staticLongPucchConfigEcpri:staticLongPucchConfigEcpriLoner\_t(see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15468\_replaced([11514029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zJfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15463\_replaced([11514001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

and into **staticLongPucchConfigEcpri:staticLongPucchConfigEcpriL1sw\_t which is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message.\*\*\*\*

This structure is used in  **UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw  message.**

**staticLongPucchConfigEcpri:staticLongPucchConfigEcpriL1sw\_t**structure content:\*\*\*\*

If UlCell\_SetupReq.eCpriStaticConfig.staticLongPucch is set to True, L2PS fills this structure with information about the Long PUCCH allocations. L1H uses this structure, to create 2 or 4 eCPRI FCP sections per c\_eAxC (per UCI allocationConfig info is not used to create FCP).

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Type** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |

**3.2.4.2.2.2.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11514041`)

eCpriPucchResourceAllocation structure
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**eCpriPucchResourceAllocation structure**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **eCpriPucchResourceAllocation structure is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**

Into **eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15471\_replaced([11514051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zKvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner(see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15463\_replaced([11514001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message and **staticLongPucchConfigEcpriLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15468\_replaced([11514029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zJfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) structure**\*\*\*\*

and into **eCpriPucchResourceAllocationL1sw which is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw(see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message and **staticLongPucchConfigEcpriL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_226\_replaced([11514021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) structure.**\*\*\*\*

**eCpriPucchResourceAllocationL1sw structure**

This structure is used in **UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw message and** staticLongPucchConfigEcpriL1sw structure**.**\*\*\*\*

If UlCell\_SetupReq.eCpriStaticConfig.staticLongPucch is set to True, L2PS fills this structure with information about the Long PUCCH allocations. L1H uses this structure, to create 2 or 4 eCPRI FCP sections per c\_eAxC (per UCI allocationConfig info is not used to create FCP).

Structure used to describe a contiguous Long PUCCH allocation. This structure is reused 2 times per c\_eAxC for Dedicated PUCCH (lower/upper), and optionally additional 2 times c\_eAxC for Common PUCCH (lower/upper). If Common PUCCH is not scheduled, numPrb of Common PUCCH is set to zero (meaning no transmission).

| >>>startPrb | u16 range[0, 272] | start PRB allocation of a contiguous  long PUCCH allocation. The allocation covers all PUCCH resources (multiple UCIs) that are allocated in a part of bandwidth. | Loki/Thor [CB016075-K] / GPU [End CB016075-K] : u16 range[0, 272] |  | CB006466-H / FGCR-8750 |
| >>>numPrb | u16 range[0, 273] | number of PRBs for a contiguous long PUCCH allocation. Default: zero | Loki/Thor [CB016075-K] / GPU [End CB016075-K] : u16 range[0, 273] |  | CB006466-H / FGCR-8750 |
| >>>eCpriSectionId | u16 | eCpriSectionId (regionId) for a contiguous long PUCCH allocation, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5163 | Loki/Thor [CB016075-K] / GPU [End CB016075-K] : u16 |  | CB006466-H / FGCR-8750 |

##### 3.2.4.2.2.3 pucchAreaBoundaries structure

###### 3.2.4.2.2.3.0-1 pucchAreaBoundaries structure Loki/Thor/Odin (ID: 11514060)

**3.2.4.2.2.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11514064`)

pucchAreaBoundaries structure
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**pucchAreaBoundaries**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **pucchAreaBoundaries structure is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**

Into **pucchAreaBoundaries:pucchAreaBoundariesLoner\_t (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15503\_replaced([11514071](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zL_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15463\_replaced([11514001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

and into **pucchAreaBoundaries:staticLongPucchConfigEcpriL1sw\_t which is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw(see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message.\*\*\*\*

**pucchAreaBoundaries:staticLongPucchConfigEcpriL1sw\_t**

This structure is used in  **UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw  message.**

This structure is used when UL PRB muting is enabled. it shows boundaries of the pucch resources combination for dedicated and common pucch resources.  If frequency hopping is enabled, there shall be up to 4 dedicated pucch boundaries and 4 common pucch boundaries.

If UL PRB muting is disabled, all pucchBoundary structures shall be set to 0 and numPucchBoundaries set to 0 as well.

**[CB009055-5G-A] This structure shall be supported in Thor**. [END CB009055-5G-A]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Type** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| >>numPucchBoundaries | u8 | The actual number of pucch area that L2 composes. | **[CB008941-A]** **Loki** **[End CB008941-A] /** **[CB009055-5G-A]** **Thor** **[End CB009055-5G-A]** enum u8{0,1,2,3,4,5,6,7,8} |  | CB008941-A |
| >>pucchBoundary | StaticFixedSizedArray[8] | This indicates a PUCCH area of dedicated PUCCH region combination and common PUCCH area. Four PUCCH boundaries are for common PUCCH and four PUCCH boundaries are for dedicated long PUCCH combination. Describing frequency domain contiguously for each dedicated PUCCH erea is in order to reduce the fragments in uplane.     For example, dedicated long PUCCH takes 14 symbols and L2 configure the startPRB of each boundary.  Upper part SR occupies PRB10~PRB12, HARQ occupies PRB15~PRB18, pCSI occupies PRB21~PRB28; Lower part SR occpies PRB98~PRB100, HARQ occpies PRB 92~PRB95, pCSI occupies PRB78 ~PRB89.   If frequency hopping is enabled for all PUCCH resources.   After hopping, the post hop half occupy 7 symbols.  upper-post-hopping: SR: PRB98 ~ PRB100 HARQ: PRB92~PRB95 pCSI: PRB82~PRB89 lower-post-hopping: SR: PRB10~PRB12 HARQ: PRB15~PRB18 Pcsi: PRB21 ~PRB32   Above all are all configured by L2 according to the combination of all dedicated PUCCH regions.   Then there are four dedicated PUCCH areas. **pucch boundary 1{startPRB=10, numOfPrb=19, startSym=0,numOfSym=7}** **pucch boundary 2{startPRB=82, numOfPrb=19, startSym=7,numOfSym=7}** **pucch boundary 3{startPRB=78, numOfPrb=23, startSym=0,numOfSym=7}** **pucch boundary 4{startPRB=10, numOfPrb=23, startSym=7,numOfSym=7}** Four PUCCH areas at most per symbol (including two common pucch boundaries and two dedicated pucch boundaries), one is for the upper area and the other is for the lower area (upper-pre-hopping, lower-post-hopping, lower-pre-hopping, upper-post-hopping). | **[CB008941-A]** **Loki** **[End CB008941-A] /** **[CB009055-5G-A]** **Thor** **[End CB009055-5G-A]** |  | CB008941-A |

###### 3.2.4.2.2.3.0-2 pucchAreaBoundaries structure Loner (ID: 11514067)

**3.2.4.2.2.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11514071`)

pucchAreaBoundaries structure
**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **pucchAreaBoundaries structure is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**

Into **pucchAreaBoundaries:pucchAreaBoundariesLoner\_t which is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15463\_replaced([11514001](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MI_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

and into **pucchAreaBoundaries:staticLongPucchConfigEcpriL1sw\_t (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14907\_replaced([11514064](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0zLfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used in** UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message.\*\*\*\*

**pucchAreaBoundaries:pucchAreaBoundariesLoner\_t structure:**

This structure is used in **UlData\_PucchReceiveReqLoner message**.\*\*\*\*

This structure is used when UL PRB muting is enabled. it shows boundaries of the pucch resources combination for dedicated and common pucch resources.  If frequency hopping is enabled, there shall be up to 4 dedicated pucch boundaries and 4 common pucch boundaries.

If UL PRB muting is disabled, all pucchBoundary structures shall be set to 0 and numPucchBoundaries set to 0 as well.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Type** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| >>numPucchBoundaries | u8 | The actual number of pucch area that L2 composes. | **Loner:** Not supported |  | CB008941-A |
| >>pucchBoundary | StaticFixedSizedArray[8] | This indicates a PUCCH area of dedicated PUCCH region combination and common PUCCH area. Four PUCCH boundaries are for common PUCCH and four PUCCH boundaries are for dedicated long PUCCH combination. Describing frequency domain contiguously for each dedicated PUCCH erea is in order to reduce the fragments in uplane.     For example, dedicated long PUCCH takes 14 symbols and L2 configure the startPRB of each boundary.  Upper part SR occupies PRB10~PRB12, HARQ occupies PRB15~PRB18, pCSI occupies PRB21~PRB28; Lower part SR occpies PRB98~PRB100, HARQ occpies PRB 92~PRB95, pCSI occupies PRB78 ~PRB89.   If frequency hopping is enabled for all PUCCH resources.   After hopping, the post hop half occupy 7 symbols.  upper-post-hopping: SR: PRB98 ~ PRB100 HARQ: PRB92~PRB95 pCSI: PRB82~PRB89 lower-post-hopping: SR: PRB10~PRB12 HARQ: PRB15~PRB18 Pcsi: PRB21 ~PRB32   Above all are all configured by L2 according to the combination of all dedicated PUCCH regions.   Then there are four dedicated PUCCH areas. **pucch boundary 1{startPRB=10, numOfPrb=19, startSym=0,numOfSym=7}** **pucch boundary 2{startPRB=82, numOfPrb=19, startSym=7,numOfSym=7}** **pucch boundary 3{startPRB=78, numOfPrb=23, startSym=0,numOfSym=7}** **pucch boundary 4{startPRB=10, numOfPrb=23, startSym=7,numOfSym=7}** Four PUCCH areas at most per symbol (including two common pucch boundaries and two dedicated pucch boundaries), one is for the upper area and the other is for the lower area (upper-pre-hopping, lower-post-hopping, lower-pre-hopping, upper-post-hopping). | **Loner:** Not supported |  | CB008941-A |
| >>>startPrb | u16 range[0, 272] | This just indicate start of dedicated long PUCCH resrouce, either of SR/HARQ/pCSI. It is not the start of of the alloction for a particular UE. | **Loner:** Not supported |  | CB008941-A |
| >>>numOfPrb | u16 range[0, 273] | Number PRB of all dedicated long pucch combination.   Note: numOfPrb = 0, it means this structure is not used | **Loner:** Not supported |  | CB008941-A |
| >>>startSymbol | u8 | First PUCCH symbol for each half if frequency hopping is enabled. First PUCCH symbols for upper or lower part PUCCH if frequency hopping is disabled.   For supported configrations, see 5G\_L1\_17221\_replaced([11455229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAhQ4vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Loner:** Not supported |  | CB008941-A |
| >>>numOfSymbol | u8 range[0, 14] | Number of PUCCH symbols.   For supported configrations, see 5G\_L1\_17221\_replaced([11455229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAhQ4vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note: if numOfSym = 0, it means structure is not used | **Loner:** Not supported |  | CB008941-A |
| >>eCpriConfigLoner | structure, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15540\_replaced([11514135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aO_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) | Structure for eCPRI configuration purpose.   **Note: this structure doesn't exist in IF code.** **Note: this structure is for descriptive purpose only and its elements are directly inserted here in the implementation.**   **Note: L2 shall set patternId to 0 since this resource is just used by RF eframer** | **Loner:** Not supported |  | CB008941-A |

**[End CNI-132817]**

##### 3.2.4.2.2.8 eCpriPucchFcpAllocConf structure

**3.2.4.2.2.8.0-1**  (ID: `11514167`)

eCpriPucchFcpAllocConf structure
**eCpriPucchFcpAllocConf**

**[Before CB006991-C-UPD002]**

This structure is used in *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq message. It shall be filled when "staticLongPucch" is set to false in* UlCell\_SetupReq. Starting PRB and number of PRB may differ from the fields of *PucchResourceAllocationConfig (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_218\_replaced([11514105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aNPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if RIM-RS detection is requested in the same slot.*\*\*

**[End CB006991-C-UPD002]**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Parameter | Type | Description | L1 HW Support | Restricted parameter combination | First Feature |
| fcpStartPrbc | u16 range[0, 272] | Starting PRB of the PUCCH resource for eCPRI FCP section generation. | Loner/Loki/Thor: Not supported |  | CB006991-C |
| fcpNumPrbc | u16 range[1, 273] | Number of PRB of the PUCCH resource for eCPRI FCP section generation. | Loner/Loki/Thor: Not supported |  | CB006991-C |
| secondHopStartPrbc | u16 range[0, 272] | If frequency hopping is enabled (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_218\_replaced([11514105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aNPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), starting PRB of the PUCCH resource for the second hop for eCPRI FCP section generation. | Loner/Loki/Thor: Not supported |  | CB006991-C |
| secondHopNumPrbc | u16 range[1, 273] | If frequency hopping is enabled (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_218\_replaced([11514105](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR1aNPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), number of PRB of the second hop for eCPRI FCP section generation. | Loner/Loki/Thor: Not supported |  | CB006991-C |

[CB006991-C-UPD002]

This structure is not used by L1SW.

[End CB006991-C-UPD002]

[CB009029-5G-A] Parity from CB006991:

This requirement also applies to Thor.

[End CB009029-5G-A]

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

#### 3.2.4.2.3 PUCCH Receive Response PS message

##### 3.2.4.2.3.1 PUCCH Receive Response PS message content

###### 3.2.4.2.3.1.0-1 PUCCH Receive Response PS message content Loki/Thor/Odin/GPU (ID: 11514178)

**3.2.4.2.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11514182`)

PUCCH Receive Response PS message content
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message content:**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages.**

On Loner platforms, **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15484\_replaced([11514193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs  continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw.***\****\*

Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner or **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

**UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |

###### 3.2.4.2.3.1.0-2 PUCCH Receive Response PS message content Loner (ID: 11514189)

**3.2.4.2.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11514193`)

PUCCH Receive Response PS message content
**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages.**

On Loner platforms, **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner (5G\_L1\_IF\_15484\_replaced([11514193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs  continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*

Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner or **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

**UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |

##### 3.2.4.2.3.2 PucchRespPsMeas structure

###### 3.2.4.2.3.2.0-1 PucchRespPsMeas structure Loki/Thor/Odin/GPU (ID: 11514203)

**3.2.4.2.3.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11514207`)

PucchRespPsMeas structure
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**PucchRespPsMeas:**

This structure is used in **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs message.**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **PucchRespPsMeas structure is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different structures.**

Into **PucchRespPsMeasLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15488\_replaced([11514216](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BSfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is use in** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15484\_replaced([11514193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BRPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message\*\*\*\*

and into **PucchRespPsMeasL1sw which is use in** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_221\_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) message.\*\*\*\*

**PucchRespPsMeasL1sw:**

This structure is used in **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw message.**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Type** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| >>shortTermTaMetric | s16 | **[Before 5GC000580-F] Position of the highest peak over the measured energy in time domain per antenna.** **[End 5GC000580-F]** **[5GC000580-F] Position of the highest peak over the measured energy in time domain.** **[End 5GC000580-F]**   Time unit set to Tsμ where Tsμ = (1/2μ) Ts Ts = 32.5 ns as per 3GPP.   Field not used by L2-PS **[5GC001389-A] The field is used by L2-PS if pucchFormat = 2 and actTimeAlignExtension is true** **[End 5GC001389-A]** **[5GC000885-A] The field is used by L2-PS if pucchFormat = 3 and actTimeAlignExtension is true** **[End 5GC000885-A]**   **TDD:** μ = 1 for FR1 and μ = 3 for FR2. **[Before PR497643]** For FR1 the range is [-32…112] For FR2 the range is [-32…110] **[End PR497643]** See also F2: 5G\_L1\_17439\_replaced([11457371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fArB1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), F3: 5G\_L1\_17428\_replaced([11458028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAuFLfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).   **FDD:** Time unit set to Ts as μ = 0, thus (1/2μ)Ts = Ts. **[5GC000836-B] The value is set to 0 for PUCCH short format 0.** **[End 5GC000836-B]** **[5GC000836-I] For PUCCH short format 2, refer to 5G\_L1\_17439\_replaced([11457371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fArB1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** **[End 5GC000836-I]**   **[Before PR497643][PR444525] The invalid value −32768 indicates that the corresponding shortTermTaPeakAmp is out of the allowed range or that a PUCCH F0 or that a PUCCH F2 with less than 3 PRBs is received.** [End PR444525][End PR497643]***\** \*[PR497643] The invalid value −32768 indicates that the shortTermTaMetric is out of the allowed range or that a PUCCH F0 or that a PUCCH F2 with less than 3 PRBs is received.** [End PR497643]***\** \*[5GC000885-A] Additionally, the invalid value -32768 indicates that a PUCCH F1 is received. An invalid indication is no sent with reception of PUCCH F3. All PUCCH F3 configurations fulfil always the minimum requirement to provide a valid shortTermTaPeakAmp.** **[End 5GC000885-A]** **[CB009543-B]** When FDD supercell is activated, if L2 send the IE isServingSubcell=false in **UlData\_PucchReceiveReqL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_216\_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to L1, L1 shall not processing decode data and return back this shortTermTaMetric invalid value (-32768) to L2, refer to 5G\_L1\_18355\_replaced([11454256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAcYW_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** **[End CB009543-B]** | Loki/Thor [CB012115-IA] /Odin [End CB012115-IA] [CB016075-K] / GPU [End CB016075-K] : [Before PR497643] [Before PR444306] [Before 5GC000580-F] array [2] of s8 range[-32, 112] [5GC000580-F] s8 range[-32, 112] [End 5GC000580-F] [PR444306] s16 range[-32, 112] [End PR444306] [PR497643] s16 range[-80...80] [End PR497643] |  | 5GC000836-B 5GC000836-I 5GC000580-F 5GC001389-A PR444306 PR444525 PR497643 5GC000885-A 5GC002006-A |

#### 3.2.4.2.4 PUCCH Receive Response HarqD message

##### 3.2.4.2.4.1 PUCCH Receive Response HarqD message content

###### 3.2.4.2.4.1.0-1 PUCCH Receive Response HarqD message content Loki/Thor/Odin/GPU (ID: 11514250)

**3.2.4.2.4.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11514255`)

PUCCH Receive Response HarqD message content
**[Before CNI-132817]**

**UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message content:**

**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages.**

On Loner platforms, **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15494\_replaced([11514265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oUfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD  continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw.***\****\*

Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner or **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

**UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Type** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |

###### 3.2.4.2.4.1.0-2 PUCCH Receive Response HarqD message content Loner (ID: 11514261)

**3.2.4.2.4.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11514265`)

PUCCH Receive Response HarqD message content
**[CNI-132817]**

Important note:

The old **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message is split from CNI-132817 onwards into two different messages.**

On Loner platforms, **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner (5G\_L1\_IF\_15494\_replaced([11514265](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oUfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and on all other platforms **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD continues as** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_224\_replaced([11514255](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BUvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*

Thereby, the L1-L2 interface is split into two different versions, one for Loner and one for all other platforms. This way, these messages can be updated for new platforms while the size of the Loner based messages can be kept within the hardware limit of the FPGA. Wherever **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD is referenced in the specifications, from CNI-132817 onwards, based on the platform in question, either the** UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner or **UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw message definition should be used.**\*\*\*\*

**UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Type** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |

**prachBeamProbingResult\_t**

### 3.2.4.4 Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request

#### 3.2.4.4.0-9 Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request Precise Positioning (ID: 11514362)

**3.2.4.4.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `11514376`)

Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request
Unexpected Exceptions:

In case of unexpected exception, no response message is returned.

---

#### 3.2.4.4.0-10 Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request UlData_SrsReceiveReq message (ID: 11514379)

**3.2.4.4.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `11514383`)

Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request
**UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message content:**

**[5GC001868-C, 5GC001868-D, 5GC001868-E]**

5G-L1-UL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support UlData\_SrsReceiveReq in **Loki L1 HW**

**[End 5GC001868-C, 5GC001868-D, 5GC001868-E]**

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] 5G-L1-UL and 5G-L2-PS shall also support UlData\_SrsReceiveReq in** Thor L1 **[End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]**\*\*\*\*

The request contains three configuration structures:

(1) a srsSuMimo structure used for SRS\_SUMIMO purposes,

(2) a srsBm structure used for SRS\_BM purposes,

~~(3) a srsSuMimo structure used for FSS FDM scheduling purposes.~~

**[CB009459-A]**

(3) a srsBwv structure used for Subband Beamweight vector calculation.

**[End CB009459-A]**

Boolean flag IEs srsSuMimo and srsBm indicate if the request in given slot is used for SRS\_SUMIMO, SRS\_BM, or both. In case only one of the purposes is valid in a given slot, the structure for the unused purpose is left empty.

**[CB009459-A]**

Boolean flag IE srsBwvEnable indicates if the request in given slot is used for Subband Beamweight vector calculation. If flag is set to false, the structure for the Subband Beamweight vector calculation is left empty.

**[End CB009459-A]**

**[CB009527-A]**

Boolean flag IE srsRtBfEnable indicates if the request in given slot is used for real time beamforming (SRS channel estimation in L1 UL and beams computation in L1 DL). If flag is set to false, srsRtBf structure is left empty**.**

**[End CB009527-A]**

**[CB012115-SR-IA] Shall be supported also in Odin L1 HW.**[End CB012115-SR-IA]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| **[Before 5GC001258-A] addrSrsReceiveResp** **[End 5GC001258-A]** **[5GC001258-A] srsReceiveRespClientAddress** **[End 5GC001258-A]** | u32 | EQID where *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs shall be sent* | **Loner/Loki/Thor:** u32 [CB012115-SR-IA] Odin: u32 [End CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: u32 [End CB016075-K] |  | 5GC001258-A |
| srsReceiveRespBmClientAddress | u32 | EQID where *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs shall be sent* | **Loner/Loki/Thor:** u32 [CB012115-SR-IA] Odin: not supported [End CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: Not supported [End CB016075-K] |  | 5GC001258-A |
| srsReceiveRespBwvClientAddress | u32 | EQID where *Uldata\_SrsReceiveRespBwvPs shall be sent* | **Loki:** u32 [CB012115-SR-IA] Odin: not supported [End CB012115-SR-IA] [CB016075-K] GPU: Not supported [End CB016075-K] |  | CB009459-A |

| >rnti | u16 | UE identifier (C-RNTI) of the BM resource. | **Loner/Loki/Thor:** u16 |  | CB008322-G |
| >bmUeContextIndex | u16[0 …maxPeriodicSrsBmUsers+ maxSubbandbeamformingUsers-1] | This parameter shall be considered by L1 only when SRS beam management functionality is enabled (actSrsBmCalcInL1 = true). Otherwise, the receiver shall ignore this parameter and its value shall not affect processing. bmUeContextIndex shall be a unique identifier per L1 subcell for each UE with beamforming context in L1. The index is used to reference UE-specific beamforming context within L1. The subcell-level limit is 1500 BM in total per subcell. Since maxSubbandbeamformingUsers is fixed to 16, maxPeriodicSrsBmUsers should be set to 1484, so that the sum of both parameters remains within the validated 1500 per-subcell buffer limit. |  |  | CB015122-A |
| >srsResourceInfo | u8 | This parameter shall be considered by L1 only when SRS beam management functionality is enabled (actSrsBmCalcInL1 = true). Otherwise, the receiver shall ignore this parameter and its value shall not affect processing. srsPort bitmask \* LSB 0: usageULBm + 1: resource is used for UL beam management + 0: resource is not used for UL beam management \* LSB 1: usageDLBm + 1: resource is used for DL beam management + 0: resource is not used for DL beam management \* LSB 2-3: portIndex (range: 0-3), + Indicates SRS port index when applicable + L1 shall use portIndex only for SrsBmStruct + L1 shall ignore these bits for SrsBwvStruct and SrsRtBmStruct and shall use portIdx in SrsBwvStruct and SrsRtBmStruct instead. \* LSB 4-6:  numOfSrsPortDlBm (encoded) + range [1,2,4], filled when LSB 1 is 1 (usageDLBm = 1) + In DL-related processing, L1 shall use numOfSrsPortDlBm to determine the number of SRS ports used for beam management. \* LSB 7: reserved The filling and population of srsResourceInfo (including srsPort, portIndex, and usage flags) is handled by L2. L1 shall treat this parameter as an input IE and remain agnostic to the filling logic. |  |  | CB015122-A |
| >bmUeContextOperation | u8 | This parameter shall be considered by L1 only when SRS beam management functionality is enabled (actSrsBmCalcInL1 = true). Otherwise, the receiver shall ignore this parameter and its value shall not affect processing. Operation BitMask indicating actions to be executed by L1 before performing instantaneous CoMa calculation for the current SRS schedule in the corresponding slot. Bit allocation (LSB first): Bit 0: 1 - L1 shall reset the UE UL BM long-term CoMa state and shall reset the UE UL BM valid instCoMa counter (rrmNumOfCoMa). 0 - No UL BM reset action shall be performed. Bit 1: 1 - L1 shall reset the UE DL BM long-term CoMa state, shall drop all SRS ports' instCoMa of the SRS UE ports in case multiple SRS resources are configured in different slots, and shall reset the UE DL BM valid instCoMa counter (rrmNumOfCoMa). 0 - No DL BM reset action shall be performed. Bits 2-7: Reserved |  |  | CB015122-A |
| >ignoreBm | u8 {False=0, True=1} | When set to True, the flag indicates that beam management request for this rnti shall be ignored by L1. The goal is to reduce SRS processing, however, L1 still requires the SRS resource configuration information for all the scheduled UE’s. Default value: 0 (False) | **Loner/Loki/Thor:** u8 {False=0, True=1} |  | CB013710-A |

Operation BitMask indicating actions to be executed by L1 before performing instantaneous CoMa calculation for the current SRS schedule in the corresponding slot. Bit allocation (LSB first): Bit 0: 1 - L1 shall reset the UE UL BM long-term CoMa state and shall reset the UE UL BM valid instCoMa counter (rrmNumOfCoMa). 0 - No UL BM reset action shall be performed. Bit 1: 1 - L1 shall reset the UE DL BM long-term CoMa state, shall drop all SRS ports' instCoMa of the SRS UE ports in case multiple SRS resources are configured in different slots, and shall reset the UE DL BM valid instCoMa counter (rrmNumOfCoMa). 0 - No DL BM reset action shall be performed. #### 3.2.4.4.0-14 Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request srsRtBf structure (ID: 11514438)

**3.2.4.4.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `11514442`)

Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request
**srsRtBf structure content:**

**Note: below table is only valid when RT BF is activated. In other cases, L1 shall ignore this structure.**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Parameter** | **Range** | **Description** | **L1 HW Support** | **Restricted parameter combinations** | **First Feature** |
| ceDumpGranularityInSubbands | u8 | SRS channel estimation (CE) result dump granularity. - LSB bit 7: 0 means CE result is saved in snapshot history buffer (HB) file. 1 means CE result is saved in local HB file. - LSB bit 0~6: gives the beamforming (BF) subband granularity. For example, 3 means that every third BF subband reuqires CE dump. Value 0 means no dump is needed. | **Thor: u8**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-C |
| numOfRtBfUeIndex | u8 | Number of UE indices that are configured with real time beamforming (RT BF) for subband beamfomring (SB BF) | **Thor:** **[Before CB014315-A]** **[Before CB009527-D][CB009527-B] u8[1..4]** [End CB009527-B]***\** \*[CB009527-D]** u8[1..16] **[End CB009527-D]** **[CB014315-A]** u8[1...68] **[End CB014315-A]** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-A |
| **Per ueIndex:** |  |  |  |  |  |
| >rtBfUeIndex | u16 | Unique identifier of the UE that activates SB BF   - MSB bits 0~3 are used to define BF type. Value 1 means RT SB BF. Other values are reserved. - LSB bits 0~11 are used to indicate the value of the unique identifier of current UE. Valid range is between 0 and [Before CB014315-A] 15 [CB014315-A] 67 [End CB014315-A] (maximum [Before CB014315-A] 16 [CB014315-A] 68 [End CB014315-A]UEs can support SB BF simultaneously).   Refer to 5G\_L1\_15517\_replaced([11469759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fB3UtfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). | **Thor: u16** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** | Invalid combination [5] | CB009527-A |
| >bmUeContextIndex | u16[0 … maxPeriodicSrsBmUsers+ maxSubbandbeamformingUsers-1] | This parameter shall be considered by L1 only when SRS beam management functionality is enabled (actSrsBmCalcInL1 = true). Otherwise, the receiver shall ignore this parameter and its value shall not affect processing. bmUeContextIndex shall be a unique identifier per L1 subcell for each UE with beamforming context in L1. The index is used to reference UE-specific beamforming context within L1. The subcell-level limit is 1500 BM in total per subcell. Since maxSubbandbeamformingUsers is fixed to 16, maxPeriodicSrsBmUsers should be set to 1484, so that the sum of both parameters remains within the validated 1500 per-subcell buffer limit. | Loki/Thor |  | CB015122-A |
| >srsResourceInfo | u8 | This parameter shall be considered by L1 only when SRS beam management functionality is enabled (actSrsBmCalcInL1 = true). Otherwise, the receiver shall ignore this parameter and its value shall not affect processing. srsPort bitmask \* LSB 0: usageULBm + 1: resource is used for UL beam management + 0: resource is not used for UL beam management \* LSB 1: usageDLBm + 1: resource is used for DL beam management + 0: resource is not used for DL beam management \* LSB 2-3: portIndex (range: 0-3), + Indicates SRS port index when applicable + L1 shall use portIndex only for SrsBmStruct + L1 shall ignore these bits for SrsBwvStruct and SrsRtBmStruct and shall use portIdx in SrsBwvStruct and SrsRtBmStruct instead. \* LSB 4-6:  numOfSrsPortDlBm (encoded) + range [1,2,4], filled when LSB 1 is 1 (usageDLBm = 1) + In DL-related processing, L1 shall use numOfSrsPortDlBm to determine the number of SRS ports used for beam management. \* LSB 7: reserved The filling and population of srsResourceInfo (including srsPort, portIndex, and usage flags) is handled by L2. L1 shall treat this parameter as an input IE and remain agnostic to the filling logic. | Loki/Thor |  | CB015122-A |
| >bmUeContextOperation | u8 | This parameter shall be considered by L1 only when SRS beam management functionality is enabled (actSrsBmCalcInL1 = true). Otherwise, the receiver shall ignore this parameter and its value shall not affect processing. Operation BitMask indicating actions to be executed by L1 before performing instantaneous CoMa calculation for the current SRS schedule in the corresponding slot. Bit allocation (LSB first): Bit 0: 1 - L1 shall reset the UE UL BM long-term CoMa state and shall reset the UE UL BM valid instCoMa counter (rrmNumOfCoMa). 0 - No UL BM reset action shall be performed. Bit 1: 1 - L1 shall reset the UE DL BM long-term CoMa state, shall drop all SRS ports' instCoMa of the SRS UE ports in case multiple SRS resources are configured in different slots, and shall reset the UE DL BM valid instCoMa counter (rrmNumOfCoMa). 0 - No DL BM reset action shall be performed. Bits 2-7: Reserved | Loki/Thor |  | CB015122-A |

| >symbolPosition | u8[8..13] | Parameter: starting position in the time domain **l**0. | >ceOperation | u8 | Bitmap indicates action(s) related to channel estimation (CE) for UEs that require RT beams:   - LSB bit 0: 1 means it is the first time to receive SRS I/Q sample in current SRS subband and cached SRS CE in DDR shall be cleared.  0 means it is not the first time to receive SRS I/Q sample in current SRS subband. No need to clear DDR. - LSB bit 1: indicating if BF subbands at lower PRB edge that has no SRS PRB allocation shall be filled with CE results from the closest BF subband belongs to current subband SRS resource. Refer to ~~5G\_L1\_15820\_replaced([11469882](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fB5J1_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))~~ 5G\_L2\_18709 for detailed definition. - LSB bit 2: indicating if BF subbands at higher PRB edge that has no SRS PRB allocation shall be filled with CE results from the closest BF subband belongs to current subband SRS resource. Refer to ~~5G\_L1\_15820\_replaced([11469882](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fB5J1_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))~~ 5G\_L2\_18709 for detailed definition. - LSB bit3: 1 means 5G-L1-UL shall always update latest SRS CE results per BF subband per SRS port no matter the SRS subband quality (*interferedSrsSubband and ~~dtx~~* portPower in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15279\_replaced([11514515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32evvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 0 means that if current SRS subband is detected as interfered (*interferedSrsSubband =1) or ~~DTX~~ low port power (~~dtx~~ ~~= 1~~* portPower < *srsPowerThreshold), then no need to update the latest SRS CE results for the corresponding SRS ports. In case of LSB bit0 in ceOperation is 1, this bit shall be ignored by L1 as it shall update SRS CE per BF subband per SRS port. Refer to 5G\_L1\_15853\_replaced([11507273](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fFf3efvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.****\**\*** - LSB bit 4: 0 means that correlation of channel estimation is not needed for current SRS subband and SRS port(s). Invalid value -1 should be reported in *correlation (5G\_L1\_IF\_15279\_replaced([11514515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32evvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). 1 means that CE correlation shall be computed according to 5G\_L1\_15521\_replaced([11507247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fFf3cfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*\*\* [CB012971-A] - LSB bit 5: 1  means the first time to receive SRS I/Q sample of current rtBfUeIndex after this UE is setup. L1 shall clear the middle bfsubband H buffer and dtx buffer  for user correlation. 0 means no need to clear buffer. [End CB012971-A] [CB012971-E] - LSB bit 6: 1  means SVD values shall be calculated and reported in response message UlData\_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs([11514519](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32e_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). 0 means SVD values are not required. [End CB012971-E] - Other bits are resvered. | **Thor: u8** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-A |

#### 3.2.4.4.0-15 Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs message (ID: 11514446)

**3.2.4.4.0-15.0-3**  (ID: `11514463`)

Sounding Reference Signal Receive Request
**SrsAntMeas:**

This structure is used in **UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs message to provide per receive antenna stream measurement results.**

The results could be used by L2PS for beam management purpose.

**[Before CB009363-D] [Before CB009363-A]**

In case of 2Rx, the last two elements of each array in the following table shall be filled with invalid values (see 5G\_L1\_8332\_replaced([11404019](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9RvmPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_8343\_replaced([11404327](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9S9uvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_8304\_replaced([11403756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9Qhe_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the definitions of invalid values)

**[CB009363-A]**

The size of antenna-wise measurements for SRS is extended to support C8 subcell. In case of **2Rx or 4Rx,** the last six or four elements of this array shall be filled with invalid values, respectively.\*\*\*\*

**[End CB009363-A] [CB009363-D]**

The parameters in the following table are no longer arrays. **The structure itself is changed to dynamic array.**

**[End CB009363-D]**
