A generic covariance matrix of size mxm is defined as

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a matrix labeled "CovMat". The matrix is square and appears to be of size m x m. The elements of the matrix are denoted by R followed by two indices, for example, R\_{0,0}, R\_{1,0}, etc. Some elements are also denoted with a superscript asterisk, such as R^\**{1,0}. The elements are colored differently, with purple, blue, green, black, orange, and light blue colors used for different elements. The last element in the last row and last column is colored red and is denoted as R*{m-1,m-1}.
The matrix can be represented as follows:

|  | 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 | ... | m-1 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **0** | R\_{0,0} | R^\*\_{1,0} | R^\*\_{2,0} | R^\*\_{3,0} | R^\*\_{4,0} | R^\*\_{5,0} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,0} |
| **1** | R\_{1,0} | R\_{1,1} | R^\*\_{2,1} | R^\*\_{3,1} | R^\*\_{4,1} | R^\*\_{5,1} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,1} |
| **2** | R\_{2,0} | R\_{2,1} | R\_{2,2} | R^\*\_{3,2} | R^\*\_{4,2} | R^\*\_{5,2} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,2} |
| **3** | R\_{3,0} | R\_{3,1} | R\_{3,2} | R\_{3,3} | R\_{4,3} | R\_{5,3} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,3} |
| **4** | R\_{4,0} | R\_{4,1} | R\_{4,2} | R\_{4,3} | R\_{4,4} | R\_{5,4} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,4} |
| **5** | R\_{5,0} | R\_{5,1} | R\_{5,2} | R\_{5,3} | R\_{5,4} | R\_{5,5} | ... | R^\*\_{m-1,5} |
| **...** | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... | ... |
| **m-1** | R\_{m-1,0} | R\_{m-1,1} | R\_{m-1,2} | R\_{m-1,3} | R\_{m-1,4} | R\_{m-1,5} | ... | R\_{m-1,m-1} |

Matrix CovMat is reported as the arrary CovarianceMatrixHorizontal/CovarianceMatrixVertical in 5G\_L1\_IF\_14086\_replaced([11514484](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32dfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The following mapping matrix-to-vector is used:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression enclosed in square brackets. The expression is a sequence of terms, each of the form $R\_{i,j}$, where $i$ and $j$ are indices. The terms are separated by commas and ellipses, indicating a pattern. The indices appear to follow a structured progression. The first few terms are $R\_{0,0}, R\_{1,0}, R\_{2,0}$, followed by an ellipsis and then $R\_{m-1,0}$. This suggests a row where the first index increases while the second index remains 0.
The next set of terms starts with $R\_{1,1}, R\_{2,1}, R\_{3,1}$, followed by an ellipsis and $R\_{m-1,1}$. This indicates a second row where the first index increases, and the second index is 1.
Following this, there are terms $R\_{2,2}, R\_{3,2}, R\_{4,2}$, with an ellipsis and $R\_{m-1,2}$, suggesting a third row with the second index as 2.
The expression concludes with an ellipsis and the term $R\_{m-1, m-1}$. The coloring of the terms suggests different groups or rows within the expression. The first group ($R\_{0,0}$ to $R\_{m-1,0}$) is purple. The second group ($R\_{1,1}$ to $R\_{m-1,1}$) is light blue. The third group ($R\_{2,2}$ to $R\_{m-1,2}$) is green. The final term ($R\_{m-1, m-1}$) is red.
The overall structure implies a matrix or a similar mathematical object where the indices represent rows and columns, and the expression lists elements of this structure. The use of 'm' suggests a variable dimension.
The text extracted from the image is:
[R0.0, R1.0 R2.0, Rm-1.0 R11 R2.1-R3.1 Rm-1.1 R2.2 R3.2, R4.2, Rm-1.2, Rm-1m-1][/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_527.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

In other words, the covariance matrix is reported column by column in array form, with first entry being R0,0 and last entry being Rm-1,m-1, respectively. Each entry Ri,j  is 32 bits long, consisting of respective Q(1.0.15) for real and imaginary part. Ri,j=[Q(1.0.15) real part , Q(1.0.15) imaginary part].

Note: diagonal entries are reported as complex numbers with imaginary part=0 for alignment purposes.

Note: Due to the reported CoMa from 5G-L1-UL being in format Q(1.0.15) (5GMax uses floating point format for CoMa), 5G-L2-PS needs to correct CoMa power computation during validation as indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2165.

[CB010887-A] The requirements above shall also be supported in 5G-L1-UL radio. [End CB010887-A]

[CNI-122313] RINLINE 1 support is terminated in 24R1, requirement is not valid for RINLINE 1 starting from 24R2 [End CNI-122313]

---

| >correlation | dynamic array[4] of float{[0,1],-1} | Array containing the magnitude of the correlation coefficient  between the Channel estimate (CE) vector (at the middle PRB of the middle subband using mid-PRB method) of different SRS ports at different time periods, t and t-1 (where t is the symbol(s) used for CE during report t) i.e., the difference between two consecutive reports. Array mapping to SRS ports is as follows:   correlation [0]: correlation between SRS port #0 CE(t) and SRS port #0 CE(t-1).  (first *portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).* correlation [1]: correlation between SRS port #1 CE(t) and SRS port #1 CE(t-1).  (second *portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).* ... correlation [3]: correlation between SRS port #3 CE(t) and SRS port #3 CE(t-1).  (fourth *portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*   Invalid value is set to -1.  Used for debuggability purposes and also for L2 to decide if the UE should be configured as SB BF UE | **Thor: dynamic array[4] of float{[0,1],-1}**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-A |
| >srsResourceIdentity | u8 | Parameter used by L2PS. Same value as received in srsRtBf structure (5G\_L1\_IF\_ 15277) for the same UE. | **Thor: u8**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-A |
| >numInterferedBfSubband | dynamic array[4] of u16 | Number of beamforming (BF) subbands that are detected with high interference of each SRS port. If corresponding function is disabled (*rdSubbandInterferDetFlag*= 0), then value 0 shall be reported. Array mapping to SRS ports is as follows: **numInterferedBfSubband [0]: Number of BF subbands for the first SRS port.  (first* portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).* numInterferedBfSubband [1]: Number of BF subbands for the second SRS port.  (second *portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).* ... numInterferedBfSubband [3]: Number of BF subbands for the fourth SRS port.  (fourth *portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).* | **Thor: dynamic array[4] of u16**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-B |
| >interferedSrsSubband | dynamic array[4] of u8 | Current SRS subband interference status of each SRS port. Value 1 means the corresponding SRS port is detected with high interference. Value 0 means the corresponding SRS port is detected with low or no interference. If corresponding function is disabled (*rdSubbandInterferDetFlag*= 0), then value 0 shall be reported. Array mapping to SRS ports is as follows:\*\*   interferedSrsSubband [0]: SRS subband interference status for the first SRS port  (first portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).   interferedSrsSubband [1]: SRS subband interference status for the second SRS port  (second portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). ... interferedSrsSubband [3]: SRS subband interference status for the fourth SRS port  (fourth portIndex in srsRtBf structure, 5G\_L1\_IF\_15277\_replaced([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). | **Thor: dynamic array[4] of u8**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-B |
| >timingOffset | s16[-80..80] | **[CB009527-E] Timing offset as position of the highest energy peak over the measured time window. Unit is set to Ts1 where Ts1 = (1/2) \* Ts with Ts = 32.5 ns.**   **Note: functionality of this field is disabled when *rdSrsCeToEnabledFlag is false (5G\_L1\_16903\_replaced([11470466](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fB_QffvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), reported value is random  invalid value -32768. Functionality of this field is activated when \*rdSrsCeToEnabledFlag is true. Valid value shall be reported.****[End CB009527-E]*\* | **Thor: s16[-80..80]**   **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB009527-E |
| >numOfUeCorrelation | u8[0...8] | Number of APS correlations calculated with current UE Note: Maximum number of APS correlations per SRS symbol is 8 for frame structure 5GC01116, otherwise maximum number of APS correlations per SRS symbol is 4. | **Thor: u8[0..8]** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB012971-A |
| **Per ueCorrelation:** |  |  |  |  |  |
| >>rtBfCorrUeIndex | u16 | Unique identifier of the UE which correlation to be calculated with current UE. Same as corresponding UE identifier defined in srsRtBf structure in UlData\_SrsReceiveReq message.   - MSB bits 0~3 are used to define BF type. Value 1 means RT SB BF. Other values are reserved. - LSB bits 0~11 are used to indicate the value of the unique identifier of current UE. Valid range is between 0 and 15 (maximum 16 UEs can support APS correlation calculation). Note: After CB014315-A APS correlation shall be used when subbandBfSwitchAlgo = Basic. | **Thor: u16** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** | Invalid combination [1][2] | CB012971-A |
| >>RNTI | u16 | UE identifier(C-RNTI) of the UE which correlation to be calculated with current UE. | **Thor: u16** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB012971-C |
| >>correlationValue | float{[0...1],-1} | APS correlation value calculated between current UE and UE with identifier ‘rtBfCorrUeIndex’. Invalid value is set to -1.  Used for debuggability purposes and also for L2 to decide if the UE should be configured as SB BF UE | **Thor: float{[0...1],-1}** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB012971-A |
| >singularValue | dynamic array[4] of float32 | Calculated singular values for the UE. If the LSB bit6 of ceOperation in srsRtBf structure([11514442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is 1, singular value for the UE shall be calculated and report to L2. Valid singular value shall be non-negative. All negative values are invalid. Any unsuccessful calculation (algorithm failure to converge) shall report value 0 for the failed singular values. Refer to [12769676](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_6xkjl4fhEfCrqOdGJPoCRA). | **Thor: dynamic array[4] of float32** **Loner/Loki/AiC: not supported.** |  | CB012971-E |

| sfn | u16[0..1023] | System frame number (SFN) corresponding to the TTI in which UlData\_SrsBeamCalcUlReceiveReq was issued and the associated SRS resource was processed. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| slot | u8[0..79] | NR slot index corresponding to the same TTI as indicated by the SFN field for the associated UlData\_SrsBeamCalcUlReceiveReq. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| subcellId | u8[0..ulSubcellIdMax] | subcellId is defined as an unrestricted subcell identifier within L1. subcellId is defined by [12706122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Ag3FwGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). ulSubcellIdMax value is defined by [12706124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_5ne9sGGPEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). L1 shall accept any value in the range [0...ulSubcellIdMax]. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| numBeamCalculationUE | u8[1..32] | Number of beam calculation UE entries. This field is not an encoded parameter in the interface message. It represents the number of elements contained in the dynamic array srsBeamCalcUe carried in this request message. The actual transmitted parameter is: srsBeamCalcUe: srsBeamCalcDlUeResp\_t[l1\_common::SRS\_MAX\_NUM\_BEAM\_CALC\_UE] attributes {dynamic\_alloc} The number of beam calculation UE entries shall be derived from the length of the srsBeamCalcUe dynamic array. SRS\_MAX\_NUM\_BEAM\_CALC\_UE (which is 32 here), defines the maximum supported number of UE beam calculation entries. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| **Per Beam Calculation UE:** |  |  |  |  |  |
| >rnti | u16 | UE identifier (C-RNTI) of the beam calculation UE | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| >bmUeContextIndex | u16[0 … maxPeriodicSrsBmUsers+maxSubbandbeamFormingUeNumber-1] | This parameter shall be considered by L1 only when SRS beam management functionality is enabled (actSrsBmCalcInL1 = true). Otherwise, the receiver shall ignore this parameter and its value shall not affect processing. bmUeContextIndex shall be a unique identifier per L1 subcell for each UE with beamforming context in L1. The index is used to reference UE-specific beamforming context within L1. The subcell-level limit is 1500 BM in total per subcell. Since maxSubbandbeamformingUsers is fixed to 16, maxPeriodicSrsBmUsers should be set to 1484, so that the sum of both parameters remains within the validated 1500 per-subcell buffer limit. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| >numUlBeamToCalc | u8:1,2,4,8 | The number of UL beams to be calculated (numUlBeamToCalc) shall be determined based only on the following two parameters: \* numberOfRxBeamforming \* rdSuUeReceiverSize (L2 R&D parameter) The value of numUlBeamToCalc shall be set according to the following rules: 1. If numberOfRxBeamforming = 2, then numUlBeamToCalc shall be set to 1. 2. If numberOfRxBeamforming = 4, then numUlBeamToCalc shall be set to 2. 3. If numberOfRxBeamforming = 8, then numUlBeamToCalc shall be set to 4. 4. If numberOfRxBeamforming = 16 and rdSuUeReceiverSize = 16, then numUlBeamToCalc shall be set to 8. 5. If numberOfRxBeamforming = 16 and rdSuUeReceiverSize = 8, then numUlBeamToCalc shall be set to 4. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| >beamSetTypeBm | enumerate:0,1 | 0- NORMAL\_BEAM\_SET -L1 shall report beam gains for the DFT normal beam set only. -Beam selection shall be performed using the DFT normal beam set only. 1- NORMAL\_AND\_TAPERING\_BEAM\_SET -L1 shall report beam gains for both the DFT normal beam set and the taper beam set. -Beam selection shall be performed using the DFT normal beam set only. -Taper beam gains are reported for information purposes but are not used for beam selection. POWER\_SAVING\_BEAM\_SET is not supported in this interface. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |

BEST\_BEAM\_ONLY (0): L1 shall calculate and report only the best DL beam. BEST\_AND\_PAIRED\_BEAMS (1): L1 shall calculate and report the best DL beam together with its paired beams [2]. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |
| >beamSetTypeBm | enumerate:0 or 1 or 2 | 0- NORMAL\_BEAM\_SET -L1 shall report beam gains for the DFT normal beamset only. -Beam selection shall be performed using the DFT normal beamset only. 1- NORMAL\_AND\_TAPERING\_BEAM\_SET -L1 shall report beam gains for both DFT normal beamset and taper beamset. -Beam selection shall be performed using the DFT normal beamset only. 2- POWER\_SAVING\_BEAM\_SET -L1 shall report beam gains for the power saving beamset. -Beam selection shall be performed using the power saving beamset only. | **Loki/Thor** |  | CB015122-A |

## 3.2.5 UL logging Procedures

### 3.2.5.0-1 UL logging Procedures Document Owner Tao-Kerry Huang (ID: 11514679)

### 3.2.5.1 buffer freeze indicate for L1 suspicious events

**3.2.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `11514687`)

buffer freeze indicate for L1 suspicious events
Messages:

UlData\_DiagnosticInd

Purpose:

L1 informs L2 to freezes it's buffers.

Precondition:

L1 starts the collection and stores IQ data on BTS storage after NR L1 Event Triggered.

Addressing:

The message is sent to the L2 address which is got in the phase of UL address navigation.

For the L2 address, L2 should not create one new address. L2 should using the existing address which is one of the PUSCH/PUCCH/SRS response address.

Description:

[CNI-76719] L1 informs L2 immediately about the event trigger:

For IQ data capture, when L1 suspicious event is triggered and before L1 indicate OAM for BTS Snapshot. L1 informs L2 immediately by sending UlData\_DiagnosticInd (for UL Loner and Loki) to L2. L2 shall freeze L2 trace buffers after receiving this message [END CNI-76719].

Expected Exceptions:

Synchronized L2 Traces and L1 IQ sample collection

UlData\_DiagnosticInd message content:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Field Name | Format | Range | Description | First Feature |
| indType | UINT\_8 | { 0: Freeze ,   } | Indicate message purpose and origin | CNI-76719 |

---

### 3.2.5.2 Uplink Fast Antenna snapshot Request

**3.2.5.2.0-5**  (ID: `11514715`)

Uplink Fast Antenna snapshot Request
**UlData\_FastAntennaSnapshotResp message content:**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Field Name | Format | Range | Definition | **First Feature** |
| status | UINT\_8 | **[Before CNI-76719]{ 0:NoError** 20: DefaultError } **[CNI-76719]** { 0:NoError 3:OutOfSequence 4:ServiceBusy [PR840468] 5:~~MissingMemory~~ [End PR840468] 6:DataNotAvailable 7:MinTimeRejection [PR840468] 8~~:RxUnderflow~~ 9:~~HwError~~ 10~~:DMAError~~ 11~~:FileError~~ 12:~~HaltOnResourcesLimit~~ [End PR840468] 13:SubcellNotConfigured 20:DefaultError } **[End CNI-76719]** | Positive / negative acknowledgment Refer to BTSC\_L1\_Req\_4892 for the details. | CNI-51355 |

[Before PR840468]

On reception of this message with positive acknowledgement (status=0: NoError),  L2 component shall increment an internal counter assoiated to request of this abnormal event.

if L1 response is not OK, L2 shall wait for a while e.g. 120 seconds before triggering next abnormal event.

[PR840468]

if L1 response status = 0 indicate NoError, L2 shall increment an internal counter assoiated to request of this abnormal event.

if L1 response status = 4, 7 indicate busy status, L2 shall set a wait timer before triggering next abnormal event.

if L1 response status = 3, 6, 13, 20 indicate configration error, L2 shall not set a wait timer.

[End PR840468]

Above requirement shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW

**[CB009552-E] This requirement shall be supported for** RINLINE2 **[End CB009552-E]**\*\*\*\*

---

| Thor | 0 | 32 |

| Thor | 0 | 32 |

#### 3.2.6.1.4 NTAoffset

**3.2.6.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11514759`)

NTAoffset
NTAoffset as defined in 38.211 and 38.133 (FR1: 13 us, FR2: 7 us)

[Before 5GC000580-F]NTAoffset as defined in 38.211 and 38.133 for FR2: 7.015 us (i.e. 13792Tc). For FR1, there is no change and it equals to 13 us. [End 5GC000580-F]

[5GC000580-F] NTAoffset as defined in 38.211 and 38.133:

FR1: 13.02us (i.e. 25600Tc; without LTE-NR coexistence) or 20.31us (i.e. 39936Tc; with LTE-NR coexistence)

FR2: 7.015us (i.e. 13792Tc)

L1 gets its value from API\_L1SW\_CPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG (i.e. NtaOffset in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_368) (Loner CPRI)

[End 5GC000580-F]

[before PR457557][5GC000836-B][5GC000580-F]

NTAoffset is 0 for FDD (38.133 table 7.1.2-2)

[End 5GC000580-F][End 5GC000836-B][End PR457557]

[PR457557][5GC000580-F] For FDD set to:

0 (with LTE-NR coexistence) or

13.02us (i.e. 25600Tc; without LTE-NR coexistence)

[End 5GC000580-F][End PR457557]

Note 1:

NTAoffset could be calculated from:

CPRI (Loner): API\_L1SW\_CPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG

eCPRI 7-2a (Loner): API\_L1SW\_eCPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG

CPRI/OBSAI (Loki/Thor): API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_AXC\_REQ\_MSG

eCPRI 7-2a (Loki/Thor): API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_EAXC\_REQ\_MSG

[5GC001868-C] Above requirement shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-C]

[5GC001868-E] Above requirements (TDD FR2) shall be also supported in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-E]

[5GC001972-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support above requirements for NTAoffset for FDD FR1 in vDU L1 HW [End 5GC001972-A]

[CB007487-B] Above requirement shall be supported also for L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB007487-B]

[CB007487-D] Above requirement shall be supported also for L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI. [End CB007487-D]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009444-G] This requirement is applicable for RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-G]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE 1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE 1 HW is not supported since 24R2

[End CNI-122313-A]

#### 3.2.6.2 Common L1/L2 timing reference

**3.2.6.2.0-1**  (ID: `11514791`)

Common L1/L2 timing reference
11514791:
Common L1/L2 timing reference
11514791:
Common L1/L2 timing reference
11514791:
Common L1/L2 timing reference
11514791:
Common L1/L2 timing reference
11514791:
Common L1/L2 timing reference
11514791:
Common L1/L2 timing reference
**UL Timings:**

On L1 side, the timing handling is computed thanks to BCN counter (N1:40 bits + N2:24 bits).

The DL NR-slot boundary is explicitly defined to be the DL NR-slot boundary at the 5G-NB antenna.

The DL NR-slot boundary will be used as time reference also for UL NR-slot  
[Before CB013338-B]  
and all UL associated messages.

[CB013338-B]

DL NR-slot boundary will be used as time reference for UL request messages.

UL NR-slot boundary will be used as time reference for UL response messages.

[End CB013338-B]

As per definition (see 38.211, subclause 4.3.1), the UL NR-slot boundary is advanced of NTAOffset (see ~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_279~~ 5G\_L1\_IF\_282\_replaced([11514759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5roPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Receive request messages timings definition:

The maximum delta time between UL receive request message and the channel/signal being transmitted by the 5GUE and received by the 5GNB is:

* A us + T\_BB1ToAnt us (non-mixed FH mode)
* T6aMax(UL) utu (mixed FH mode)

The minimum delta time between UL receive request *message and the channel/signal being transmitted by the 5GUE and received by the 5GNB is:*

* B us + T\_BB1ToAnt us (non-mixed FH mode)
* T6aMin(UL) utu (mixed FH mode)

Response messages timings definition:

5G-L1-UL expects to send towards 5G-L2-PS/LO at the soonest (C - NTAOffset + T\_AntToBB1) us and at the latest (D - NTAOffset + T\_AntToBB1) us after the starting boundary of the NR-slot of concern the UL receive response messages, the reference being the DL NR-slot boundary.

Values of A, B, C and D are specified in the following requirements:

* On **Loki and** Thor [CB011026-A] in CPRI and eCPRI-7-2a **[End CB011026-A]:**\*\*\*\*
* For TDD FR1: 5G\_L1\_IF\_14384\_replaced([11514812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rp_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For TDD FR2: 5G\_L1\_IF\_285\_replaced([11514834](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rqvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For FDD: 5G\_L1\_IF\_286\_replaced([11514847](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rrPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**[CB011026-A]**

* On **Thor in eCPRI-7-2e:**
* For TDD FR1: 5G\_L1\_IF\_15166\_replaced([11514926](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR6St_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**[End CB011026-A]**

* On **Loner:**
* For TDD FR1: 5G\_L1\_IF\_14407\_replaced([11514822](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rqPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For TDD FR2: 5G\_L1\_IF\_285\_replaced([11514834](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rqvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* For FDD: 5G\_L1\_IF\_14409\_replaced([11514854](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rrfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

**[Before CB013338-B]**

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with a small, light gray rectangle in the bottom center containing the text "UL channel".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_584.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**[CB013338-B]**

For Loki and Thor in non-mixed FH mode:

Transmission Window is specified with detailed values.  
Reception window is adjusted according to transmission window by taking transportation delay into account.

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a sequence diagram illustrating a communication flow between different network entities, likely in a 5G system. The diagram depicts messages and timing windows exchanged between "5G-L2-PS", "5G-L1-UL (BB)", "Rd", and "Ru".
Here's a breakdown of the elements:
**Entities:**
\* **5G-L2-PS:** Likely represents the 5G Layer 2 Protocol Stack.
\* **5G-L1-UL (BB):** Likely represents the 5G Layer 1 Uplink Baseband.
\* **Rd:** A network entity, possibly a Radio Unit or a similar component.
\* **Ru:** Another network entity, possibly a Radio Unit or a similar component.
\* **5G-L2-LO:** Likely represents the 5G Layer 2 Lower Layer.
**Messages and Timing Windows:**
\* **BCN = 0 frameStart (for SFN = 0):** Indicates the start of a frame, with a Broadcast Channel (BCN) value of 0 and SFN (System Frame Number) also being 0.
\* **UL Req TX window:** An uplink request transmission window.
\* **T56\_Min, T56\_Max:** Minimum and maximum timing values related to the UL Req TX window.
\* **UL Req RX timing:** An uplink request reception timing window.
\* **A, B:** Points in time or signals.
\* **1 (T\_BB1ToAnt):** A timestamp or signal indicating transmission from BB1 to Antenna.
\* **B' = B - T56\_Max, A' = A - T56\_Min:** Calculations based on timing values.
\* **Ru (NTAOffset):** An offset value related to the Ru entity.
\* **T\_AntToBB1:** Timing from Antenna to BB1.
\* **7: UL Resp TX window:** An uplink response transmission window.
\* **UL Slot:** A time slot for uplink transmission.
\* **C, D:** Points in time or signals.
\* **4 (T78\_Min, T78\_Max):** Minimum and maximum timing values.
\* **C' = C + T78\_Min, D' = D + T78\_Max:** Calculations based on timing values.
\* **8: UL Resp RX timing:** An uplink response reception timing window.
The diagram shows a sequence of events where an uplink request is transmitted and received, followed by an uplink response. Timing parameters like T56 and T78 are used to define the windows for these transmissions and receptions. The calculations involving A, B, C, and D with these timing parameters suggest precise synchronization and timing control within the system.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-03051617.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

**[End CB013338-B]**

**[CB008124-B, CB009055-5G-A]Pusch decoding time (D) is used to compute configured grant timer in L2-PS. Refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14592.** [End CB008124-B, CB009055-5G-A]\*\*\*\*

**[5GC000579-C] Fixed transport delay in the diagrams is replaced by variable *T\_AntToBB1 (for UL direction). See ~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_121~~ 5G\_L1\_IF\_122 for description and values before 5GC000579-C and starting from 5GC000579-C.\*\*[End 5GC000579-C]***\*\*

In response to UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, following messages are sent:

* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs
* UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD (sent when *nANPucch from UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is > 0)*

In response to UlData\_PuschReceiveReq, following messages are sent:

* UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs
* UlData\_PuschReceiveRespLo
* UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqU

**[5GC000885-A] UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD (sent when *numOfUciAckBits from UlData\_PuschReceiveReq is > 0) \*\*[End 5GC000885-A]***\*\*

In response to UlData\_PrachReceiveReq, following message is sent:

* UlData\_PrachReceiveInd

In response to UlData\_SrsReceiveReq, following message is sent:

* UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs

**[Before CNI-98319]**

**[5GC002056-BA]**

No message is sent in a response to UlData\_EmptyReceiveReq.

**[End 5GC002056-BA]**

**[CNI-98319]**

UlData\_EmptyReceiveReq message is removed.

**[End CNI-98319]**

**[CB008249-A]**

In response to UlData\_RimReceiveReq, following message are sent:

* 1st UlData\_RimReceiveRespPs if delay-managed symbols are considered for RIM
* 2nd UlData\_RimReceiveRespPs if NDM SRS symbol is considered for RIM

**[End CB008249-A]**

**Note:**

**[IFL100308-C]**

**1.  Value of T\_BB1ToAnt shall be configured by OAM and L1(BB) could calculate it from (see details :5G\_L1\_IF\_123\_replaced([11513234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRvTmfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :**

For CPRI (Loner):  **T\_BB1ToAnt = dlFiberLengthCompensationOffset (common)**from API\_L1SW\_CPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG\*\*\*\*

For CPRI/OBSAI (Loki/Thor): **T\_BB1ToAnt = pathDelay (downlink) from API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_AXC\_REQ\_MSG**

For eCPRI ***\*T\_BB1ToAnt = tDlAdvanceUp, where* \*tDlAdvanceUp** of downlink channel PDXCH calculated from:***\****\*

eCPRI 7-2a (Loner): API\_L1SW\_eCPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG (common)

eCPRI 7-2a / 7-2e (Loki/Thor): API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_EAXC\_REQ\_MSG (downlink)

2. Value of T\_AntToBB1 shall be configured by OAM and L1(BB) could calculate it from:

For CPRI (Loner):  T\_AntToBB1 = ulFiberLengthCompensationOffset (common) from API\_L1SW\_CPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG

For CPRI/OBSAI (Loki/Thor): T\_AntToBB1 = pathDelay (uplink) from API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_AXC\_REQ\_MSG

For eCPRI T\_AntToBB1=receiveWindowClose, where receiveWindowClose is calculated from :

eCPRI 7-2a (Loner): API\_L1SW\_eCPRI\_DELAY\_CONFIG\_REQ\_MSG (common)

eCPRI 7-2a / 7-2e (Loki/Thor): API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_EAXC\_REQ\_MSG (uplink)

**[End IFL100308-C]**

**[CB014054-G]**

For Thor CPRI and eCPRI 7-2a in the Mixed FH Mode T\_AntToBB1 shall be calculated according to [12699682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_KTA8gFzSEfCPFofqMEsORA).

For timing diagram of Loki and Thor in mixed FH mode, please refer to [13395613](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_vv6o1gcpEfGozuGzRUXHpg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

**[End CB014054-G]**

**[End CB009028-5G-A]**

### 3.2.6.3 Transportation Delay

**3.2.6.3.0-1**  (ID: `12704246`)

Transportation Delay
L1->L2 transportation delay definition:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| T78\_Min | T78\_Max |
| 0 | 20us |

For reference point 7 and 8 definitions, please refer to “Figure 2 Timing reference points for CPRI and eCPRI” in  BTS\_E2E\_Timing\_Architecture.docx, see: [12739660](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_SKdS8XmnEfCiUemk-K-C4g)

For L2->L1 transportation delay definition T56\_Min and T56\_Max, please refer to [12698062: L2->L1 transportation delay definition](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_B6s3QlyREfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

| UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqD | N/A |  |  |  |
| UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs | N/A |  |  |  |

**Note 1: In case of PUCCH scheduling with UCI bits only (no HARQ bits, *nANPucch from *UlData\_PucchReceiveReq is 0),*UlData\_PucchReceiveRespHarqD message is not sent.***\*\*

~~**Note 2: In case there are multiple *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs messages requested by a single *UlData\_SrsReceiveReq, the timing window applies to all related*UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs messages.***\*\*~~

~~**Note 3: This message is sent only when *numOfUciAckBits from UlData\_PuschReceiveReq is > 0.***~~

~~**Note 5: In high load scenario, PRACH may go as high as 1500 [us]**~~

[CB013338-B]

Note2: Separaration of "high load" and "low load" for value "D" is obsoleted, higher value is chosen to secure both cases.

Note3: for definition of T56\_Min and T56\_Max, please refer to [12698062: L2->L1 transportation delay definition:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_B6s3QlyREfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)  
            for definition of T78\_Min and T78\_Max, please refer to [12704246: L1->L2 transportation delay definition:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LTwqUWBgEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[End CB013338-B]

**Note 4: The maximum value of pucchSlotOffsetMax/puschSlotOffsetMax/srsSlotOffsetMax determines the value of A [us]**

Above requirement (TDD FR2) shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW

At the soonest timing boundary, denoted as C, shall be 0. The L1 shall send the response message as soon as processing is complete without introducing any artificial delay.

### 3.2.6.7 NDM (Non-delay managed) SRS timing

**3.2.6.7.0-6**  (ID: `11514900`)

NDM (Non-delay managed) SRS timing
For NDM SRS, each NDM SRS eAxC stream with a non-zero occasionDelay and/or receiverDelay value has a reception window end given by receptionWindowClose=T34\_max.

[CB010332-B] The same boundary applies when NDM SRS is used for Precise Positioning in Thor. [End CB010332-B]

Informative Text: the maximum delay, from SRS symbol, is computed in 5G-L1-UL as receptionWindowClose+occassionDelay+receiverDelay.

[CNI-122313]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313]

---

* The time origin, **t=0, is the start of the DL slots at air time as described in 5G\_L1\_IF\_282\_replaced([11514759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5roPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**
* **NTAoffset is defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_282\_replaced([11514759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5roPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**- {A,B,C,D} from above table.**

**- T\_BB1ToAnT (See** Note 4) and **T\_AntToBB1 (See** Note 5).***\****\*

**Note:**

1. This message is sent only when *numOfUciAckBits from UlData\_PuschReceiveReq is > 0.*
2. **In case there are multiple *UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs messages requested by a single *UlData\_SrsReceiveReq, the timing window applies to all related* UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs messages.***\*\*
3. **fhCpWindowOpen(*channel) and \**fhCpWindowClose(*channel) are the boundaries of C-plane message reception window on eCPRI-7-2e FH interface. fhCpWindowOpen(\*channel) can have negative value. Ta4\_min\_cp and Ta4\_max\_cp are defined in "eCPRI LL Split U-Plane Application Layer Specification" § 5.1.12 (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_14660\_replaced([11518734](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSTURfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Its value depends on the response message type.***\*\*\*\*
4. **T\_BB1ToAnt = tDlAdvanceUp, where** tDlAdvanceUp of downlink channel PDXCH (EPhyChannelType\_Pdxch72e) in API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_EAXC\_REQ\_MSGis calculated by OAM, see: [12739664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_F7g-8XmpEfCiUemk-K-C4g) (Reference may change in thefuture).**[PR787528] To accommondate L2 design of oneWayHWDelayDl for both UL and DL (5G\_L1\_IF\_123\_replaced([11513234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRvTmfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), it is defined for eCPRI 7-2e that tDlAdvanceUp =  oneWayHWDelayDl + 500 us. Consequently, value of A and B was reduced by 500us for all UL channels.** [End PR787528]***\****\*

5: **T\_AntToBB1 = receiveWindowClose where** receiveWindowClose is calculated by OAM, see: [12739664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_F7g-8XmpEfCiUemk-K-C4g) (Reference may change in thefuture). Since T\_AntToBB1 is common for PUSCH and SRS channels, the common reference assumed here is receiveWindowClose for PUSCH U-plane transmission under TDD FR1 (eCPRI 7.2e) configuration.\*\*\*\*

[CB013338-B]

6: for definition of T56\_Min and T56\_Max, please refer to [12698062](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_B6s3QlyREfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)  
     for definition of T78\_Min and T78\_Max, please refer to [12704246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_LTwqUWBgEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[End CB013338-B]

### 3.2.6.10 UL timings for mixed FH mode

#### 3.2.6.10.1 Overview

##### 3.2.6.10.1.0-1 Overview Mixed Fronthaul mode is the mode which support CPRI and eCPRI FH modes in the same BB cell set. For the L1 mixed FH mode shall be understand as no separation between CPRI and eCPRI for subpool configuration in L1SW configuration message. (ID: 12699602)

#### 3.2.6.10.2 UL Timing Diagram

##### 3.2.6.10.2.0-1 UL Timing Diagram 13395613: UL Timing Diagram 13395613: UL Timing Diagram 13395613: UL Timing Diagram 13395613: UL Timing Diagram 13395613: UL Timing Diagram 13395613: UL Timing Diagram 13395613: UL Timing Diagram UL timing diagram in mixed FH mode: [image-0][image_desc]The image is a timing diagram illustrating a communication protocol, likely within a 5G network. It depicts the flow of signals and timing windows between different network components, labeled as "Rd", "Ru", "5G-L2-PS", "5G-L1-UL (BB)", and "5G-L2-LO". The diagram shows two main sequences of events. The top sequence involves "Rd" and "5G-L2-PS" and "5G-L1-UL (BB)". - "Rd" initiates a process with "BCN = 0" and "frameStart (for SFN = 0)". - A "UL Req TX window" is defined for "5G-L2-PS", with minimum and maximum timing constraints "T56_Min" and "T56_Max". - A corresponding "UL Req RX timing" window is defined for "5G-L1-UL (BB)". - Several timing parameters like "T5aMax (UL)", "T5aMin (UL)", "T6aMin (UL)", and "T6aMax (UL)" are shown, indicating the duration and boundaries of these requests and responses. - "NTAOffset" and "T_AntToBB1" are also indicated, suggesting synchronization or offset calculations. - A formula is presented: "T_AntToBB1 (eCPRI) = T_AntToBB1 (CPRI) + T_offset_CPRI_eCPRI_UL". The bottom sequence involves "Ru", "5G-L1-UL (BB)", and "5G-L2-PS" / "5G-L2-LO". - "Ru" is associated with an "UL Slot". - A "7: UL Resp TX window" is defined for "5G-L1-UL (BB)". - A "8: UL Resp RX timing" window is defined for "5G-L2-PS" and "5G-L2-LO". - Timing constraints "T78_Min" and "T78_Max" are shown for these response windows. - Points labeled "C" and "D" are defined, and then adjusted to "C'" and "D'" using the "T78_Min" and "T78_Max" values, respectively: "C' = C + T78_Min" and "D' = D + T78_Max". - A circular marker with the number "4" is present, possibly indicating a step or a specific point in the process. Red text is used for timing parameters and labels.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/img-03041542.png[/image_path][/image-0] (ID: 13395613)

#### 3.2.6.10.3 T_AntToBB1 adjustment for CPRI and eCPRI cells in one subpool

**3.2.6.10.3.0-1**  (ID: `12699682`)

T\_AntToBB1 adjustment for CPRI and eCPRI cells in one subpool
For FDD Thor L1 HW in the mixed FH mode L1 Ul shall define T\_AntToBB1 for CPRI and eCPRI Cells/subCells on the base of timings for first configured via UlCell\_SetupReq message Cell/subCell in the subpool and fixed T\_offset\_CPRI\_eCPRI\_UL offset.

If the first configured via UlCell\_SetupReq message Cell/subCell in the subpool is CPRI, L1 Ul shall calculate T\_AntToBB1 in the following way:

CPRI:    T\_AntToBB1 (CPRI)  = pathDelay (uplink) from API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_AXC\_REQ\_MSG

eCPRI: T\_AntToBB1 (eCPRI) = T\_AntToBB1 (CPRI) + T\_offset\_CPRI\_eCPRI\_UL

If the first configured via UlCell\_SetupReq message Cell/subCell in the subpool is eCPRI, L1 Ul shall calculate T\_AntToBB1 in the following way:

eCPRI: T\_AntToBB1 (eCPRI) = receiveWindowClose from API2\_BBB\_CREATE\_EAXC\_REQ\_MSG (uplink)

CPRI:  T\_AntToBB1 (CPRI) = T\_AntToBB1 (eCPRI) - T\_offset\_CPRI\_eCPRI\_UL

The T\_offset\_CPRI\_eCPRI\_UL = 72us according to [12532989: (26R3 ->](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_83qDwBwcEfCQJ5daVHVkgg?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_qYdJttQ-Ee26EtvmdlGL5w "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_83qdwbwcefcqj5davhvkgg?vvc.configuration=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/cm/stream/_qydjttq-ee26etvmdlgl5w")

Note: Different T\_AntToBB1 for CPRI and eCPRI cells are needed for TTI job creation timing purpose (designed internally by L1 UL)

---

#### 3.2.6.10.4 UL timings for FDD (mixed FH mode)

**3.2.6.10.4.0-1**  (ID: `13393293`)

UL timings for FDD (mixed FH mode)
**FDD receive request message (mixed FH mode):**

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Message | UL Req Tx window (T5a) |  | UL Req Rx window (T6a) |  |
| T5aMax(UL) [us] | T5aMin(UL) [us] | T6aMax(UL) [us] | T6aMin(UL) [us] |  |
| UlData\_PucchReceiveReq | T5aMin + pucchSlotOffsetMax \* 1000 + 1030 | T5aMin + pucchSlotOffsetMin \* 1000 | T6aMin + pucchSlotOffsetMax \* 1000 + 1030 + T56\_Max - T56\_Min | T6aMin + pucchSlotOffsetMin \* 1000 |
| UlData\_PuschReceiveReq | T5aMin + puschSlotOffsetMax \* 1000 + 1030 | T5aMin + puschSlotOffsetMin \* 1000 - 650 | T6aMin + puschSlotOffsetMax \* 1000 + 1030  + T56\_Max - T56\_Min | T6aMin + puschSlotOffsetMin \* 1000 - 650 |
| UlData\_PrachReceiveReq | T5aMin + 1030 | T5aMin | T6aMin + 1030 + T56\_Max - T56\_Min | T6aMin |
| UlData\_SrsReceiveReq | T5aMin + srsSlotOffsetMax \* 1000 + 1030 | T5aMin + srsSlotOffsetMin \* 1000 | T6aMin + srsSlotOffsetMax \* 1000 + 1030 + T56\_Max - T56\_Min | T6aMin + srsSlotOffsetMin \* 1000 |

**FDD receive response message (mixed FH mode):**

Mechanism is same as in non-mixed FH mode, for timing table please refer to: [12705126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_urP-4GC5EfCLrcnPCspVyQ)  
TX window is defined as [T\_AntToBB1 + C,  T\_AntToBB1 + D],  
RX window is defined as [T\_AntToBB1 + C', T\_AntToBB1 + D']  
For T\_AntToBB1 in mixed FH mode, please refer to: [12699682](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_KQvroFzSEfCPFofqMEsORA)

Note 1: T5aMin is configured by CP-RT to L2, while T6aMin is configured by OAM to L1 via L1Config\_SetL1TimingReq message..

Note 2: T5aMin and T6aMin shall each be assigned a unique value per timing domain. These values are defined for the downlink PDCCH channel; other channels shall take it as reference if need to use different values, DL request message timing window could refer to: [12577980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_JzpO0TCyEfCRMdP0Nuo3Hg) .

Note 3: pucchSlotOffsetMax/ pucchSlotOffsetMin please refer to: [11514733](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5EoPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

puschSlotOffsetMax/ puschSlotOffsetMin please refer to: [11514747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5EovvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

srsSlotOffsetMax / srsSlotOffsetMin please refer to: [11514753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5Eo_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

Note 4: T56\_Min/T56\_Max, please refer to: [12698062](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_B6s3QlyREfCPFofqMEsORA)

Note 5: The value of T5aMin(UL) and T6aMin(UL) are defined based on an offset to T5aMin and T6aMin, the offset takes T\_L1\_processing\_DL\_CPRI = 750us as reference, which is defined here: [12532989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_83qDwBwcEfCQJ5daVHVkgg),  generally the value is calculated like:

T5aMin(UL) = T5aMin – B(DL) + B(UL)  
T5aMax(UL) = T5aMin – B(DL) +A(UL)

T6aMin(UL) = T6aMin – B’(DL) + B’(UL)  
T6aMax(UL) = T6aMin – B’(DL) +A’(UL)

Here B(DL) and B'(DL) is value B/B' of DlData\_pdcchSendReq.

11514945:
UL buffering
11514945:
UL buffering
Receive request messages on UlData interface shall indicate whether corresponding UL signals are to be processed in real time or non-real-time from UL buffer. The indication is contained in structure defined in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_264.

Receive request messages for both real time (non-delayed) and non-real-time (delayed) processing shall follow air interface timing, i.e. timing defined for real time processing in this section 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_273.

Receive response messages for delayed UL processing shall follow air interface timing with the delay of M slots, where M is the difference in slots between slotForNrtProcessing/sfnForNrtProcessing and slot/sfn from respective receive request message as shown in the graph below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a black and white diagram illustrating a timeline with several horizontal arrows indicating durations or intervals. There are two solid green arrows and two dashed green arrows. The solid arrows are positioned above the dashed arrows. The first solid arrow starts on the left and extends to the right. The second solid arrow is positioned further to the right and also extends to the right. The first dashed arrow starts to the left of the second solid arrow and extends to the right, overlapping with the second solid arrow. The second dashed arrow starts to the left of the first dashed arrow and extends to the right, also overlapping with the first dashed arrow and the second solid arrow. Below the arrows, there are two shaded gray rectangles, one to the left and one to the right, which appear to represent events or periods of time. To the far left, there is a thin vertical line. The diagram appears to be a visual representation of scheduling, sequencing, or time-based relationships between different elements. There is no discernible text in the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_609.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where:

A is the soonest allowed time when message can be received by 5G-L1-UL (excluding fiber delay) for the NR-slot n, counted from the beginning of the slot. Value is specified in the respective requirement of a given message.

B is the latest allowed time when message can be received by 5G-L1-UL (excluding fiber delay) for the NR-slot n, counted from the beginning of the slot. Value is specified in the respective requirement of a given message.

C is the soonest allowed time when response message can be sent by 5G-L1-UL (excluding NTAOffset and fiber delay) for the NR-slot n, counted from the beginning of the slot. Same values are assumed for the non-delayed and delayed case, only the reference DL NR-slot changes (slot n for non-delayed and slot n+M for delayed case).

D is the latest allowed time when response message can be sent by 5G-L1-UL (excluding NTAoffset and fiber delay) for the NR-slot n, counted from the beginning of the slot. Same values are assumed for the non-delayed and delayed case, only the reference DL NR-slot changes  (slot n for non-delayed and slot n+M for delayed case).

Values of A, B, C and D are specified in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_280.

UlData\_xReceiveReq represents any of the following messages: UlData\_PuschReceiveReq, UlData\_PucchReceiveReq, UlData\_PrachReceiveReq, UlData\_SrsReceiveReq.

UlData\_xReceiveResp represents any of the following messages UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs/Lo/HarqU, UlData\_PucchReceiveRespPs/HarqD, UlData\_PrachReceiveInd, UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs.

- Rx Front End (FE):

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$L\_{kRx FE} = \sum\_{1}^{n\_{res\_{L1}} instance} L\_{kRx FERes}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_614.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

For PUCCH F3, 3 types of latencies are encountered at L1 level:
- Demapper Level and L1 Low Latency [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation reads: $L\_{demapper+L1Low} = 125 \mu s$. The text is black and appears to be on a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_617.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
- Rx Front End (FE):
   [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$L\_{kRx FE} = \sum\_{1}^{n\_{res\_{L1}} instance} L\_{kRx FERes}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_617.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]
  Where [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "n\_resL1\_instance" in a stylized font. The text is dark gray and appears to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_617.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the number of PUCCH F3 resources per L1 instance.
o For every PUCCH F3 resource
 2 Rx FE: k=2
[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in text. The formula defines a variable $L\_{2Rx FE\_Res}$ using a piecewise definition based on the value of `CodeRate`.
The formula is as follows:
$L\_{2Rx FE\_Res} = \begin{cases} (\max{F3(\text{CodeRate, Modulation}) \times \text{UCI}*{\text{bits}}, 10}) \text{ µs when CodeRate} \le 0.25 \ 10 \text{ µs when CodeRate} > 0.25 \end{cases}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_617.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]
 4 Rx FE: k=4 hence[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "L4Rx FE" in a blurry, light-colored font against a white background. The text is horizontally aligned.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_617.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]
 [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula presented in a piecewise format. The formula defines a variable $L*{4Rx FERes}$ based on the value of $CodeRate$.
The formula is as follows:
$$
L\_{4Rx FERes} =
\begin{cases}
\max{F3(\text{CodeRate}, \text{Modulation}) \times 1.3 \times UCI\_{\text{bits}}, 13} \, \mu\text{s} & \text{when } \text{CodeRate} \le 0.25 \
13 \, \mu\text{s} & \text{when } \text{CodeRate} > 0.25
\end{cases}
$$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Interfaces\_file\_617.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]

#### 3.2.6.15.3 UlData_SrsReceiveReq, UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs, UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs procedure

**3.2.6.15.3.0-3**  (ID: `11515265`)

UlData\_SrsReceiveReq, UlData\_SrsReceiveRespPs, UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs procedure
(Moved to 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_280)

Timing of UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs

5G-L1-UL shall send the UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs towards 5G-L2-PS at the soonest (430 – NTA\_offset + T\_AntToBB1) us and at the latest (1000 – NTA\_offset + T\_AntToBB1) us after the starting boundary of the NR-slot of concern of the corresponding UlData\_SrsReceiveReq. In case there are multiple UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs messages requested by a single UlData\_SrsReceiveReq, the timing window applies to all related UlData\_SrsReceiveRespBmPs messages.

Note: Timing of UlData\_SrsReceiveReq is defined in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_303.

[5GC001868-C] Above requirement shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-C]

---

### 3.2.6.16 eCPRI UL Control Messages for Simplified Control

**3.2.6.16.0-3**  (ID: `11515312`)

eCPRI UL Control Messages for Simplified Control
If the generation of the eCPRI fast control packets is shared with 5G-L1-DL, then 5G-L1-UL shall buffer the fast control packets for Uplink to be dispatched in the transmission window based on tUlAdvanceCp and T\_NTA\_offset with respect to the starting symbol (see 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_311).

[5GC001868-A] Above requirement shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW [End 5GC001868-A]

[5GC002190-C] Above requirement shall be supported also in vDU L1 HW [End 5GC002190-C]

---

### 3.2.6.17 Fault management and defence mechanism

#### 3.2.6.17.0-1 Fault management and defence mechanism The description of actions to be taken by 5G-L1-UL when the UlData_SrsReceiveReq message is received out of its expected reception timing window is provided in: Loner: ~~reference [11]~~ 'Late arrival messages management for ABIL 5G19B', see: 12739685 . Loki: ~~reference [13]~~'BB L1 Synchronization for ABIO/ABIN for Release L1_5G20B', see: 12739652 . Source: 5G_L1_9572_replaced( 11459335 ), 5G_L1_9573_replaced( 11459355 ) (ID: 11515320)

### 3.2.6.18 UL Message TX Timestamping

**3.2.6.18.0-1**  (ID: `12705529`)

UL Message TX Timestamping
For the following uplink L1-L2 messages:

* ~~UlData\_PuschRecieveReq~~
* UlData\_PuschReceiveReqL1ru
* UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqDL1sw
* UlData\_PuschReceiveRespHarqUL1sw

Transmitter shall set timestamping for each message.  
Receiver shall record tx timestamp when a message is out of window.

TX timestamping mechanism is common for uplink and donwlink, please refer to: [12705476: TX timestamping mechanism](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_4GBU8GEhEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[PR851184] Not necessary to set tx timestmping for UlData\_PuschRecieveReq. [End PR851184]
